Diplomatic and Consular Documents Not to Use "Acting" Titles

(Nanjing) Regulations on the appointment of public officials stipulate that public officials who have not been formally recommended should be assigned as acting officials first. Some of our country's diplomatic and consular personnel stationed abroad are also acting officials. However, when using official documents in the host country, the title "Acting" often causes misunderstandings in various countries. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has repeatedly received reports from various embassies and consulates and has submitted a request to the Executive Yuan for a flexible approach. In the future, embassies and consulates will not use the title "Acting" when issuing official documents to foreign countries. (Eleventh, Special Dispatch)

Judicial Yuan Clarifies Ambiguities in Real Estate Pledge Registration

(Nanjing) The Tianjin District Court requested the Judicial Yuan to clarify ambiguities in the effectiveness of real estate pledge registration. The explanation is as follows: Regarding real estate pledge and property rights that existed as customary property rights before the implementation of the Property Rights Section of the Civil Code, they are not subject to the provisions of the Property Rights Section of the Civil Code in accordance with the Implementation Law of the Property Rights Section of the Civil Code. If registration is made in accordance with the Real Estate Registration Regulations, it still has the effect of establishing a claim. If it occurred after the implementation of the Property Rights Section, it is not a property right prescribed by law. Therefore, in accordance with Article 757 of the Property Rights Section of the Civil Code, it cannot be created and cannot have the effect of establishing a property right through registration. This is an instruction for your information. (Eleventh, Special Dispatch)

Legislative Yuan's Commerce Committee Schedules Discussion on Insurance Industry Law

(Nanjing) Regarding the issue of joint Sino-foreign ventures, most members of the Legislative Yuan believe that our country's resources urgently need to be developed. Joint Sino-foreign ventures should not be opposed as long as they do not harm our sovereignty. However, public utilities such as electricity and water should be closed to foreign investment to protect sovereignty. It was also decided that in the future, when drafting legislation, each committee of the Legislative Yuan should formulate its own regulations in accordance with this principle when encountering issues involving this matter. The Commerce Law Committee of the Legislative Yuan is drafting the Insurance Industry Law, which involves many joint Sino-foreign ventures, and has scheduled a meeting for the fourteenth to discuss the issue and review the draft Commercial Registration Law. (Eleventh, Central News Agency dispatch)

Because the evidence was conclusive, Yu was ordered to be executed by firing squad at 7:00 a.m. on the eleventh. (Eleventh, Central News Agency dispatch)

Current Affairs Commentary

Protecting Children and Removing Cruelty - Heng

丨Feelings Inspired by the Compassionate Children's Society's Request to Sanction Child Abuse丨

Recently, cases of women abusing children have been reported in newspapers from time to time. For example, the case of Zhang Aizhen, a dancer in this city, abusing her six-year-old adopted daughter, Zhang Xiaobao, and the case of Chen Xiangjun, a prostitute in Tianjin, abusing her seven-year-old maid, Lianxi, are the most prominent. These two young girls were not born to Zhang and Chen. It is not surprising that they are abused and played with for personal pleasure. The most shocking thing is the case reported in the newspapers not long ago of a woman with the surname of someone, who superstitiously believed that her own son was fated to be in conflict with her, actually dismembered him and abandoned him in the wilderness. However, this kind of inhumane event is only mentioned in terms of those who are discovered. In fact, there are probably many that are not discovered. After all, the abuse of maids was very common in the old society, and infanticide was even more common in years of famine. There are also occasional reports of deaths due to parents' superstition, so although there are not many such inhumane and cruel acts reported in newspapers, the seriousness of the problem should not be taken lightly. According to yesterday's report, the Compassionate Children's Society has put in considerable effort to protect maids through legislation, and the recent revision of the new criminal law also emphasizes child protection. It can be seen that society has paid considerable attention to these issues. European and American countries have even legislated to protect animals and do not allow them to be abused. How much more so should people not be subjected to cruel treatment and harmed in their physical and mental development? Therefore, the efforts of the Compassionate Children's Society and the vision of the legislative authorities are commendable actions.

However, protecting children through legislation is only a symptomatic treatment. To achieve a fundamental cure, further action seems necessary. The abuse of children is a manifestation of cruelty, and cruelty can be inflicted everywhere. It is not necessary to violate the criminal law before harming children. Therefore, what is needed here is the removal of cruelty. As for infanticide, which is the result of natural disasters, the power of the law is powerless, so there is no need to discuss it in detail. As for those who suffer from superstition, the fundamental solution lies in the popularization of education, which is also self-evident. However, what is the way to remove this cruelty? The answer is to explore the root causes of the formation of cruelty.

In recent years, psychologists have explained many abnormal human psychologies. The most prominent are Sigmund Freud of Austria, Altred Adler, and Carl Jung of Switzerland. According to Freud's view, psychological disorders are mostly due to the suppression of sexual desire, while Jung believes that psychological abnormalities are not limited to the suppression of sexual desire. The suppression of all other desires can lead to selfishness and cruelty. Now, looking at the real cases of Zhang Aizhen and Chen Xiangjun, the cruelty of these two to maids does not seem to be caused by the lack of sexual desire. After all, these two are dancers, so Freud's theory does not seem to apply. Jung's theory is also vague. From the reporter's point of view, Adler's theory is the most able to explain the psychology of these two people. Adler believes that cruelty, prejudice, jealousy, violence, frenzy, love of destruction, schadenfreude, and other psychologies stem from a feeling of inferiority. The feeling of inferiority is caused by the fact that one's position is inferior to others, and one is not valued, resulting in self-pity and resentment, and thinking about ways to take revenge. As a result, cruelty and other eccentric behaviors arise. Adler further said that the reason why this kind of psychology is more common in women than in men is that men still have a better social status than women in today's society. The views of the psychologists who have emerged in England and America are also mostly the same. They all say that all kinds of human desires, which have been obstructed for a long time, and accumulated in the heart, will inevitably lead to mental disorders and eccentricity. Knowing this, the reason why Zhang and Chen abuse maids can be suddenly understood. The background and circumstances of these two must also be unsatisfactory.

Since the cause is clear, the way to deal with it is naturally to eliminate the cause. After all, the use of the law has its limits and can only be applied to what has already happened, not to prevent it from happening. Therefore, it can be regarded as a symptomatic treatment, but it cannot be said to be a fundamental cure. From the perspective of the theories of the aforementioned psychologists, the fundamental solution seems to lie in seeking the satisfaction of life's desires in order to restore those with abnormalities to their normal state. However, things in the world are limited, how can everyone be satisfied? Therefore, Adler believes that it is better to cultivate a heart of love for others and for the group through education. This method has considerable value, but it is probably very difficult to achieve quick results. After all, the power of reason and thought to dominate life is often not as great as that of faith and emotion. Therefore, we believe that in these places, there should be a kind of religious-style influence that is in line with modern life to reconcile them. Then, the concept of self can be slightly removed, the psychology of loving others and the group can be enhanced, and unnecessary desires can be slightly suppressed. In this way, these cruel acts and all eccentric, criminal behaviors can be reduced day by day, and the effect will be greater than not educating and punishing them.

British Government Plans to Change the Organization of the Beijing Consulate

Foreign Secretary Simon responded that they were currently discussing changes to the British Consulate General in Nanjing so that the British Ambassador could go to Nanjing as needed. He believed that the changes to the Consulate had not yet been completed. (Eleventh, Reuters)

Japanese Policy, Pacific Crisis Latent

British-American Cooperation to Maintain Peace

Smuts' Remarks Gain American Sympathy

Japan Should Abandon Militarism

Lyttons Speech Resonates

(New York) South African Minister of Justice General Smuts gave a speech on February 9 in the capital of South Africa, discussing the Greater East Asiaism advocated by Japan, advocating that Britain and the United States should establish an agreement to protect Pacific security. According to the New York Times correspondent in Washington, the State Department is extremely satisfied with Smuts' proposal. According to some officials in the State Department, the United Kingdom and the United States have almost implemented cooperation on Far Eastern issues. The relationship between the United Kingdom and the United States is historically closer than it is now, but it is regrettable that the war debt issue has not been resolved. If the war debt issue is not resolved, the United States will inevitably feel slightly unhappy with the United Kingdom. (Eleventh, Havas)

(Washington) Sir Lytton gave a speech in the United States today, saying that if Japan is unwilling to jointly maintain world peace, then the blood shed by millions of people in the previous war would be in vain. The only result obtained from the previous war was that the countries have promised future peace. Lytton advocated that the whole world should ask Japan to recognize this fact and ask it not to give people the bad impression of militarism. Lytton loudly said that unless Japan can calm down and look around the world's current situation and change its policy, the current peace system will inevitably collapse completely. Lytton admitted that Japan's handling of the Manchurian Incident should be given considerable forgiveness in terms of economic relations. Lytton believes that Japan regards Manchuria as a place to release its population and its lifeline. However, the United Kingdom and other countries in the world believe that the signing of the world peace treaty is the lifeline of international peace. Lytton further said that if all countries in the world unanimously ask Japan to join this fair agreement, then I have not seen that Japan can refuse to ignore it. If Japan can truly understand that the benefits of peace far outweigh those of war, then it will be happy to do so. Lytton continued that the League of Nations did not fail in its handling of the Manchurian Incident. The position of the League of Nations is to use criticism as a policy, and it does not use troops to implement its beliefs. Finally, Lytton believes that although Japan can develop Manchuria by peaceful means, the Japanese army must withdraw before it can maintain the goodwill of all countries in the world. (Eleventh, National)

(London) All London newspapers published in a prominent position the speech by South African Minister of Justice General Smuts, calling on the United Kingdom and the United States to cooperate to maintain the integrity of China. Today, Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito publicly condemned Russia's conspiracy in China in a speech at the Chicago Foreign Relations Society, saying that Japan's greatest fear is Russia's aggression. Japan's intervention in Manchuria and its current activities in China aim to reduce Russia's power in these two places. In the past eight years, Moscow has repeatedly sent propagandists, political commissars, and military leaders to China to plan revolutions. Japan cannot ignore this disaster. Japan's only wish for China is that China will be an independent country for a long time. Saito said that some people think that Japan's ambition is to control China. This view is really naive. Saito's words have aroused much comment. His words are obviously in stark contrast to those of General Smuts, who warned the public in Cape Town yesterday that because of Japan's policies, the Pacific is now harboring a huge crisis, and Russia, China, the United States, and the United Kingdom are all at risk of being caught in the whirlpool. All of the United Kingdom's autonomous territories are concerned about their own safety, so they want the United Kingdom and the United States to establish the closest possible cooperation. (Tenth, Reuters)

Effective Blow to Japanese Delusions: Anglo-American Cooperation

Comments from London Newspapers

(London) South African Union's former Prime Minister and current Minister of Justice, General Smuts, delivered a speech in the South African capital last Saturday, advocating for Anglo-American cooperation to safeguard the Pacific region. This morning, newspapers here have commented extensively on this significant speech. The Times stated that Japan's economic, political, and nationalistic ambitions are exacerbating the international situation, causing disturbances even more severe than those in Europe. Under these circumstances, Anglo-American cooperation is of paramount importance to world peace. Both countries adhere to the principles of individual freedom and advocate for the peaceful resolution of international disputes, rejecting war as an instrument of national policy. Given their shared stance, cooperation is essential. The [News Chronicle] stated that [Japan undoubtedly faces its own dangers and difficulties. It would be premature to assume that Japan will never accept sound and sympathetic diplomacy. However, observing recent events, it would be too late to assert that Japan will inevitably embrace sound and sympathetic diplomacy. Japan is currently pursuing a dream of a vast empire. The only effective way to awaken it is through strong Anglo-American cooperation.] The [Daily News] stated that [The whole world must keep a close eye on the rising tides on the Pacific coast. Those devoted to world peace, like General Smuts, should recognize that the most practical way to achieve peace is through direct negotiations, urging Japan to honor its recent pledges. What are these pledges? Namely, Japan's abandonment of the Washington Naval Treaty and its lack of intention to engage in a naval arms race.] (Havas Dispatch, 11th)

(London) The Manchester Guardian commented on General Smuts' speech, expressing strong support, stating that the League of Nations has already achieved significant results. The current priority should be to allow Germany equal status based on universal disarmament, enabling Germany to rejoin the League of Nations. Then, the League of Nations can devise solutions to more serious disputes. Regarding the future of the Pacific, the newspaper advocates for Anglo-American cooperation to maintain peace in the Far East and to gain the support of various Far Eastern countries through peaceful means.

It would be difficult to succeed, and so forth. (Havas Dispatch, 11th)

US Alliances with Other Countries Not Permitted by Public Opinion

Senator Borah's Statement

(Washington) Senator Borah responded today to the proposal by South African Minister of Justice General Smuts in Cape Town, stating that the United States cannot enter into any alliances to maintain peace in the Pacific. According to Mr. Smuts, the clouds of war in the Pacific are perilous; therefore, he suggested Anglo-American cooperation for security. Borah criticized, "[General Smuts exaggerates the clouds of war in the Pacific. He suggests forming a military alliance with the United States, according to his own intentions. The United States faces difficulties in forming any alliances with other countries. General Smuts may not understand the public will of the American people, who generally disapprove of such alliances or special understandings. And the United States' foreign policy is ultimately shaped by public opinion.]" (National Dispatch, 10th)

Yamamoto Returns Home to Advise Government

The Arms Reduction Issue Regains Momentum

(Tokyo) Arms reduction delegate Yamamoto is scheduled to depart from Busan at 11:30 AM today and arrive in Tokyo at 3:30 PM tomorrow afternoon. Upon returning to Tokyo, he will provide significant advice to the government regarding arms reduction. The arms reduction issue, which had been in decline, will regain momentum after Delegate Yamamoto's return. The main points of Rear Admiral Yamamoto's significant advice are approximately as follows: 1) The opinions of the British government and the American representatives regarding Japan's notification of the abrogation of the Washington Treaty and its request for a conference; 2) The future attitude towards establishing arms equality rights; 3) Britain's attitude towards the complete abolition of offensive military forces and the basis of American opposition; 4) Concrete British arms reduction proposals obtained during private meetings with Delegate Nadolny; 5) The difficulties of reopening preliminary talks and convening the main conference, as well as the opinions of Britain and the United States. (Dentsu Dispatch, 11th)

Reports on the Current Economic Situation in China

For Reference by Foreign Minister Hirota

It seems to be a fact that China is expecting economic assistance from Japan. Shanghai is currently facing financial pressure. He believes that without self-reliance, economic recovery cannot be achieved. However, there is a need to consider emergency measures. He hopes for large-scale assistance to China. Recently, Sino-Japanese relations have returned to normalcy, which is gratifying. (Dentsu News Agency Dispatch, 11th)

The concrete measures for Sino-Japanese economic cooperation must first involve importing Japan's excellent technology into China, thereby improving the cultivation of Chinese cotton, wheat, rice, etc. If the import of expensive foreign goods is reduced and cheap and excellent Japanese goods are purchased, then Chinese trade can recover within a few years. The most important issue is loans. As a result, seven things will be considered, such as setting up loans. There are rumors that the National Government will adopt the gold standard and reduce parity, but the former is entirely out of the question, because silver is difficult to nationalize, then the latter is also hopeless. (Dentsu News Agency Dispatch, 11th)

A Thousand Puppet Police Defect

Angered by Japanese Brutality, Join the Volunteer Army

(Changchun) According to reliable sources, on the 5th of this month, a Japanese security commander in the puppet government of Huadian County, Jilin Province, had an argument with a puppet policeman. He then drew his sword and severed one arm of the Chinese puppet policeman, causing public outrage among the puppet police force. Approximately one thousand puppet police officers from the first brigade of the county immediately defected, killing the Japanese instructor, the county advisor (Japanese), and more than ten other Japanese puppet officials. Later, they planned to attack the city of Antu County, attempting to kill the enemy, and gathered at the border between Huadian and Antu counties. Upon hearing the news, the Japanese army was panicked and heavily guarded. US-Russia Trade Stagnation Does Not Affect Diplomatic Relations

(Washington) The current tense situation between the United States and Russia is only a transitional phenomenon. Ultimately, there will be a more practical solution to resolve the disputes between the two countries. This is the opinion expressed to the Associated Press reporter today by a general neutral diplomatic observer. The crux of the difficulty lies in trying to solve financial and commercial problems at the same time. The general opinion of observers is that US-Russian diplomatic relations, like French-Russian and British-Russian diplomatic relations, must undergo a long period of evolution. Furthermore, the recent stagnation of trade between the two countries reminds people of the dream of President Roosevelt after recognizing Soviet Russia, hoping for tens of millions of dollars in trade with Russia. In fact, in 1934, the United States' trade with Russia was only worth $14,866,000, and the year before it was $8,743,000. These figures are enough to prove the extent to which Americans hope to realize their dreams. However, the importance of this matter lies in its possible impact on the Far East. In other words, it is clearly unlikely that the United States and Russia will jointly deal with Japan. All of this has dispelled the predictions of the general public in 1934. Senator Borah, chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, declared today that the expression of sympathy between the United States and the Soviet Union, or the ability to change a certain policy towards Japan, is not very relevant in the current stagnation. Regarding the reduction of staff at the Soviet Union's US embassy and the withdrawal of consulates, Borah said that this move would not have a serious impact and is purely an economic issue that should not be seen as having any other purpose. (National Dispatch, 10th)

(Washington) Judging from the phenomenon, Secretary of State Hull is currently conducting negotiations on reciprocal trade agreements, and there will soon be facts to show it. Hull has felt in recent days that the United States should show other governments that while the United States is a friendly and good neighbor, it is not a country to be bullied. The United States' withdrawal of the consulate in Ynsk and the reduction of staff at the Soviet Union's US embassy are expressions of this attitude. It is said that Hull firmly believes that if the United States does not provide Soviet Russia with cash loans, then Soviet Russia will refuse to repay its debts to the United States. The cash loan that Soviet Russia intends to borrow is 100 million US dollars.

If it can be achieved, Soviet Russia will naturally take advantage of this atmosphere to conduct loans to European countries, and then blackmail the United States to obtain preferential loan conditions. Hull saw through Soviet Russia's attitude, so today, after a five-minute meeting between Hull and Soviet Ambassador to the United States Troyanovsky, he cut off negotiations. Afterwards, Hull declared that he did not hope to trade much with Soviet Russia, at least not without financial assistance from the US government. (National Press Agency Dispatch, 10th)

French Radio Station Completed

US-French Telegraph Communications Can Reach Directly

Saint-Nazaire, France. According to the Morning Post, France's most powerful radio station has been completed and will begin service on the 15th of this month. In the future, wireless telegraphs sent from France to ships sailing in the Atlantic can be received directly, and wireless communications between France and the United States will no longer need to be relayed through the United Kingdom. The main power station is located near Ceffelac and has three iron frames, each 100 meters high. Each frame has an electrical voltage of 10,000 volts. The radio station employs a total of 100 people, but only one person is needed to send and receive telegraphs. (Havas Dispatch, 10th)

Radio Transmits Images and Sounds

Watching and Listening to Speeches While Sitting in a Small Room

Successful Experiment in Berlin, Germany

A Major Revolution in Telephone Communications

)Berlin (The popularization of wireless film machines has now taken another step forward. Scientists in Berlin have created a perfect machine that can use the cathode rays of electric current to directly capture people and broadcast them. Whenever individual speeches are given in public gathering places, if the scenery is not too complicated, it can be captured and transmitted by this machine. Before this machine was invented, the transmission of wireless images required first capturing the scenery into a sound film, and then broadcasting it in separate parts. Wireless film broadcasting agencies in Berlin have been established for more than a year, and their economic support is limited to the manufacturers of receiving machines. They are also conducting various observational experiments at the same time. However, the newly invented machine is much simpler, and the number of people who purchase receiving machines in the future will inevitably increase greatly. Image and sound reception can be installed in one machine, and public speeches can be watched and listened to quietly in individual homes. Furthermore, the installation of fax machines on telephones is technically possible today, but the cost is too high and it is difficult to popularize. In the future, the national wireless film and broadcasting industry may undergo a major revolution due to the use of wires for transmission. After the use of wires to transmit scenery becomes popular, the first to benefit will be ordinary telephone communications. This type of wire was tested yesterday by Dr. Banhuezer of the German Post Office at the German Scientific Society. This was the first practical test in the world. The installation of the wire has been completed today. One end is connected to the central office of the Post Office, and the other end is connected to the wireless film transmission machine in Weizleben. It can transmit 1.2 million electrical vibrations per second, allowing ordinary news photos to have a clear outline without any light or complex dynamics. As for ordinary telephone lines, they cannot yet be used to transmit scenery at the same time, but the wires that have been successfully tested can also be used as telephone lines for transmitting sound. Therefore, it is predicted that when wireless film becomes popular in the future, the wires in all parts of the world will be replaced with new types of wires for transmitting sound and images. (National Dispatch, 10th)

One Wave Not Yet Subsided, Another Arises

The Italian-Ethiopian Border Situation Could Become Serious

Ethiopian Troops Concentrated in Walwal

Clashes Between Ethiopian and Italian Soldiers Flare Up Again

Italy Mobilizes Two Army Divisions, Darkening War Clouds

(Rome) The border dispute between Italy and Ethiopia has intensified again. An official statement declared that [Ethiopian troops are constantly concentrating near Walwal, putting pressure on Italian troops. Recently, a group of Ethiopian soldiers attacked an Italian defense force in Afdub, resulting in mutual fire. Five Italian soldiers were killed and six were injured. The Ethiopian side suffered more casualties. The Italian embassy in Addis Ababa has been ordered to lodge a formal protest.] (Havas Dispatch, 10th)

(Rome) Italy today drafted three companies of reservists due to the risk of war on the Ethiopian border. Ethiopian troops attacked Italian indigenous troops stationed south of Walwal in Italian Somaliland in the early morning of January 29th. Five Italian regular soldiers were killed and six were injured. Many Ethiopians participating in the conflict were also killed. Diplomats have been instructed to notify Ethiopian officials that Italy has suffered greatly from this kind of harassment by unofficial troops. If the Ethiopian government cannot effectively prohibit it, the Italian government will take self-defense actions. According to the official report of the incident, the government only received it today, but the above-mentioned actions have been carried out immediately. It is said that attacks similar to this one have occurred frequently recently. Details of this incident are not yet known, but it is said that the number of Ethiopian casualties in the attack was higher than that of the Italian soldiers, and they were repulsed. It is currently difficult to predict what actions the Italian government intends to take in addition to protesting to Ethiopia. However, if military action is necessary, Italy will be able to immediately deploy troops trained with modern weapons to the Ethiopian border. (National Dispatch, 10th)

(Rome) After the second clash between Italian and Ethiopian troops, Italy has mobilized two reserve divisions to prepare for reinforcement. According to a semi-official statement from the Stefani News Agency, the Italian government mobilized two reserve divisions on the 5th and 11th of this month to prevent any incident: the Berolitan Division, the 29th Division of the Province of Messina, and the Guvenaina Division, the 19th Division of the Province of Florence. Those mobilized were soldiers of the 1911 class, that is, adult soldiers born in 1911. The mobilization was quite successful. In addition, news about the Ethiopian border incident on January 29 has been issued in an official statement and published in today's newspapers to inform the public. However, the newspapers did not comment on it. (Havas Dispatch, 11th)

(Rome) Since Italy officially announced the mobilization of two army divisions today, the clouds of war have suddenly become heavy. According to sources in official circles here, unless the Italian government receives a satisfactory reply, the Italian government will issue an ultimatum to the Ethiopian government. A spokesperson for the Italian government told a reporter from the National Press Agency that the Italian government had been waiting patiently for the Ethiopian government to control the situation, but such unfortunate events still occurred, which made the Italian government unbearable. The spokesperson continued that the Ethiopian government cannot fabricate facts to deceive the world. According to general observations, the Italian government will not issue a formal declaration of war against Ethiopia. The actions of the Italian government will likely follow Japan's methods in Manchuria and Britain's methods towards Sudan, punishing Ethiopia with military force, as Italy claims that its actions are out of self-defense against Ethiopian attacks. (National Dispatch, 11th)

(Rome) An Italian Foreign Ministry spokesperson told a Reuters interviewer today that if relations between Italy and Ethiopia continue to change and become more tense than they are now, the Italian government may send a memorandum to the Ethiopian government. It is said that the currently mobilized army is a precautionary plan and will not leave Italy unless the situation becomes more serious. It is said that there are as many as 30,000 Ethiopian troops gathered at various points on the border. There are rumors outside that Italy is determined to invade Ethiopia, but judging from the current situation, it seems difficult to achieve, because Ethiopia has heavy rainfall every year from March to November, making it extremely difficult to march there. (Reuters Dispatch, 11th)

Russia-Romania Rail Through Traffic to Begin on August 1st

(Moscow) The Soviet Union and Romania railway representatives have successfully concluded discussions on through traffic issues. Comrade Gilshanov, Director of the International Transportation Bureau of the People's Commissariat of Transportation, presided over the meeting. According to Comrade Gilshanov's statement to the TASS reporter, the agreement on through traffic for Soviet-Romanian passenger and freight trains is economically important, as it will not only develop transportation between the Soviet Union and Romania but also facilitate transportation between other countries via the Soviet Union and Romania. This agreement allows Soviet passenger and freight traffic to have a shortcut when heading south to Hungary, Czechoslovakia, Albania, Yugoslavia, Austria, Italy, and southern France. At the same time, European passenger and freight can reach Persia and Afghanistan via a shorter route. The Soviet-Romanian through traffic will be implemented from August 1st after the railway bridge over the Dnieper River at Boraspol is repaired. The aforementioned meeting also had a special understanding on the bridge repair. (Tenth TASS dispatch)

Poland Develops Trade

Polish Exhibition Ship to Arrive in China in April

[Warsaw Correspondence] Poland's foreign trade saw considerable progress last year. According to precise statistics, from January to October of last year, the largest buyer of Polish goods was the United Kingdom, accounting for 24%, followed by Germany at 19%. Purchases of Polish goods by other countries such as Austria, Belgium, Denmark, and Italy also increased significantly compared to 1933. In terms of overseas trade, the largest buyer was the United States, followed by Argentina, Brazil, China, India, Mexico, South Africa, and others. It is also worth noting that Poland's overseas trade developed extensively last year. In 1933, almost all Polish goods were sold in European countries, accounting for 92.5%, while overseas trade only accounted for 7.5%. However, last year, shipments to Europe fell to 88.3%, and further to 80.3% in September, meaning that overseas trade accounted for 18.7% of the total in that month. Therefore, Poland's future business plan focuses on promoting overseas trade as much as possible while striving to improve Polish-British business relations. Trade between China and Poland also progressed last year, with Polish goods sold to China totaling approximately 2.1 million Customs Gold Units and Chinese goods sold to Poland totaling approximately 1.1 million Customs Gold Units. This is due to the success of the direct shipping route from Shanghai to Gdynia, Poland, with a special ship departing every three weeks. Furthermore, to promote the sale of Polish goods in China, the Dadalos exhibition ship plans to sail from Gdynia to Shanghai for a public exhibition, expected to arrive in Shanghai around April 20th, fully loaded with various Polish products.

Skiing Competition

Russian Soldiers Set New Record

Traveling over 4,000 Miles in 74 and a Half Days

(Moscow) A team of five soldiers from the Far Eastern Soviet Russian Army set off from Siberia on snowshoes and arrived here today after traveling 4,320 miles, setting two world records: one for completing the entire journey in 74 and a half days, and another for averaging 58 miles per day. They encountered several dangers along the way, including temperatures dropping to 72 degrees below freezing and heavy blizzards when crossing the Berga Mountains. (Tenth Reuters dispatch)

Lisbon: Portugal, which has been ruled by a military dictatorship for nine years, today re-elected its former dictator as the legitimate president. He has now been re-elected. (Eleventh National Telegram)

Conflict between Japan and Mongolia at the Halaha Temple (Harbin Correspondence)

Triangular Area is a Military Stronghold

Both Japanese and Mongolian Sides Were Prepared

However, This Time It May Be Resolved Peacefully

The Halaha River flows into the southeastern corner of Lake Buir, and the Ulshun River connects Lake Hulun and Lake Buir. Another small river, called the Chaliz River, connects the above two rivers. The triangular area between the three rivers and Lake Buir is the territory belonging to the Halaha Temple. This area has been the focus of Japanese attention since the September 18th Incident, considering it not only a fortress between [Manchukuo] and Mongolia but also of great significance in Japanese-Soviet military relations. Therefore, Mongolian soldiers trained by the Japanese are stationed at the Ganzhu Temple. The Halaha Temple incident occurred in mid-January when Japanese military instructor Major Hontani led more than ten soldiers and encountered an Outer Mongolian scout team. As a result of the conflict, several Japanese soldiers were killed or injured. On January 30th, the Japanese side dispatched a large team of soldiers from Hailar to seize the Halaha Temple. According to the Japanese side's claims and the puppet regime's propaganda, the Halaha Temple should belong to [Manchukuo] and is definitely not Outer Mongolian territory, so the Mongolian army should not forcibly enter the territory. They claim that they will not advance any further once they have driven the Mongolian army out of the territory.

However, news from Kulun, such as the statement issued by the Outer Mongolian Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Genden, stated that [the Halaha Temple and its surrounding area have belonged to Mongolian territory since ancient times and have never been under the jurisdiction of Hulunbuir. Therefore, the Outer Mongolian Republic can never agree to the occupation of the Halaha Temple by Japanese-[Manchukuo] troops and recognizes the illegal invasion of the national border by the Japanese-[Manchukuo] armies. After the Halaha Temple incident on January 24th, there was calm for several days until 8:00 AM on January 31st when the border guard team near Lake Buir discovered a unit of the Japanese-[Manchukuo] army, consisting of several military vehicles and fifty soldiers and cavalry in echelon formation, crossing the Outer Mongolian border from [Manchukuo] territory. The unit occupied Kor Obor and continued to advance into Mongolian territory. However, the Outer Mongolian border guard army, unwilling to engage in armed conflict, retreated slightly, demonstrating a calm attitude. To avoid conflict, they did not fire a single shot. They are now only building defensive positions on the shore of Lake Noring. The Outer Mongolian government, for the sake of its national rights and the restoration of peace, has forbidden the border guard army to open fire without authorization and will not hesitate to engage in peaceful negotiations in the future.]

Judging from the above statement, it seems that this matter will not escalate much. However, the Japanese troops stationed along the Middle East line are elite units from Kyoto, Nagoya, Hiroshima, and other places. Although the exact number cannot be determined, military observers believe that there are at least two and a half divisions, with a total of more than 30,000 soldiers. Therefore, it is very possible that this incident will escalate dramatically. Moreover, those young officers all want to test their skills and see who is superior to the Red Army. The other side is also quite clear about this situation and will naturally not relax their grip. They have newly mobilized five divisions of troops in the Far East, with the main units concentrated along the western border of [Manchuria].

Outer Mongolian troops in Kulun consist of mixed teams of cavalry, artillery, and machine guns, totaling approximately 20,000 soldiers, ten cannons, eight anti-aircraft guns, twenty-one bomber aircraft, and twenty-five reconnaissance aircraft. In addition, an army university, officer school, and scientific arms factory have been established in the Kulun area. With such defensive power in that vast and boundless plain, it is feared that it will not be easy for foreign forces to invade.

On the left bank of the Kherlen River, in the territory of the Chechen Khan, a large airfield has been built, hiding more than 30 bombers. In the Hentiy area, there are also 500 cavalry, an artillery team, a machine gun team, six tanks, and several military vehicles. West of the Halaha Temple, along the upper reaches of the Ulshun River, cavalry scouts frequently patrol back and forth, and automobiles often speed by, carrying out special liaison missions. In the Ikh Bulag Temple southwest of Lake Buir, there is also a regiment of infantry and a brigade of cavalry, providing considerable security. Therefore, even if the Japanese army has some ulterior motives and wants to take advantage of the situation to break in, they dare not truly engage in a head-on confrontation with the well-prepared Outer Mongolia. They will probably take advantage of Outer Mongolia's statement of peace and change course, perhaps even engaging in negotiations. (February 1st)

Japanese Build Pier in Shantou

As a Base for the Fleet and Smuggling

The Site Extends More Than Ten Zhang Into the Sea

Shantou Correspondence: The Japanese Navy rotates its patrols of the southern coast of China every season. Its fleet sails from the strategic port of Magong in Taiwan, heading directly to Shanghai, Wenzhou, Fuzhou, Xiamen, Shantou, Hong Kong, or even Guangzhou, and occasionally to Hainan Island. Every island, mountain, port, and stone on the southern coast of China, its depth, and the time and strength of the tides are thoroughly understood. The tonnage of Japanese merchant ships sailing in South China almost surpasses that of British and Norwegian merchant ships. Japanese ships arriving in Shantou have always docked on the Qilu sea, that is, the Shen Zhao Road end in front of the Japanese Consulate. The Japanese Consulate is the most magnificent building among the consulates of various countries in Shantou, with a police station and prison inside. The consulate is located in the center of the city, about 300 steps in front of the Eastern District Office, and faces the Eastern District Office across the street. Japanese warships berth at Qilu almost every day, with a rotation of garrison personnel. Officers and soldiers disembark using small motorboats or sampans, landing in the fields at the end of Shen Zhao Road near the consulate. All secret transportation activities take place here. Nearby is the Datong Ice Factory, opened by Taiwanese people, which occupies a large area. Many Japanese and Taiwanese people are concentrated here. Further ahead are the Dongying School, Boai Hospital, and Japanese Elementary School, each occupying several acres of land and capable of being used for gatherings and garrisoning troops. In particular, the Japanese Elementary School across from the Municipal Government is unusually sturdy, resembling a military camp. There are observation posts and various facilities on the corners of the building, which can communicate with ships through flag signals and lights. The number of Japanese residents scattered around Qilu has increased sharply in recent years, numbering no less than four or five hundred, but there has never been a thorough investigation, because most of the businesses they operate are of a mobile nature.

Last year, Japanese consular officials stationed in South China were summoned by the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Taiwan to hold a conference on the other side of the strait. Developing Japanese commerce in Shantou was also an important issue at the conference. Long ago, they had been considering building a pier at a suitable location along the coast to dump Japanese goods in the Chaoshan region, to facilitate the docking of merchant ships and warships and the transportation of heavy machinery and goods. Because the barge workers of the Shantou sea had been united in refusing to load and unload passengers and cargo for Japanese ships. After the Shanghai Incident of the previous year, the arrogance of Japanese residents increased, and small motorboats and barges with the Japanese flag were able to operate freely. The workers' union disintegrated invisibly, and Japanese goods were able to flow smoothly into the Chaoshan market and be sold in various counties. Initially, Taiwanese people contracted for transportation, but recently there have been many conflicts with the tax bureau's inspectors. For example, in the case of seafood, in addition to paying customs duties as required, it is also necessary to pay the seafood Kyoto donation, but Taiwanese people refuse to pay, resulting in incidents of assaulting inspectors and police chiefs. The local authorities here have adopted a policy of appeasement, and each case has been compromised, which is regrettable. The momentum of Japanese residents in Shantou is such that the pier they urgently need has now been built.

The Haitan at the mouth of Commercial Street was originally owned by the Commercial School and the Gospel Hospital, with undisputed ownership. However, five years ago, a Japanese national named Luo Bingzhang suddenly had a dispute over management with the Commercial School. This case remains unresolved to this day. It is said that Luo was acting on Japanese instructions, initiating the plan to build a pier. Today, Japanese people are again occupying land on Shen Zhao Road to build a pier, extending more than ten zhang beyond the Haitan into the sea, and the Datong Ice Factory is building it on the surface. They did not report to the Municipal Government beforehand, clearly intending to infringe on our territorial sovereignty and violating the regulations of the Municipal Government. The Public Security Bureau, based on a report from the Oka police, has lodged representations with the Japanese side.

An investigation into the actions of the Japanese in Shantou has recently attracted great attention from the authorities. For example, the Japanese previously established a Sun Dance Hall on Yushen Street, attracting people with weak wills to spy on the secrets of various agencies in the city. They also formed the Dongjiao Society, using so-called friendly language to recruit laborers, porters, boatmen, shops, and vendors from the lower classes. Each person paid a small membership fee each month. All members could use external influence to abuse their authority and resist tax collectors and inspectors, as well as avoid taxes. Initially, it was quite popular, but after the authorities paid attention to prevention, they used a different approach, operating secretly. The most obvious thing is the smuggling electric boats along the coast. Last year, the Chaozhou Customs had repeatedly seized them, but the electric boats ignored everything and even took the customs officers to Taiwan for business negotiations. We made representations, but to no effect. The next is the smuggling of goods, not paying taxes, contracting to transport them to Chaozhou and Jieyang counties in the interior for sale, and establishing warehouses. If the inspectors detained the goods, they would form an assault team to deal with them. Previously, the National Salvation Association intercepted a small boat carrying seafood and shark fins on the Wuchiao River and detained the people and goods at the National Salvation Association. The assault team even gathered from a factory in Wuchiao, carrying weapons and pistols, and made a big scene at the National Salvation Association, taking away the goods and people. Such major cases are also unresolved, so the power of the assault team has increased day by day, and the inspectors and tax collectors are no match for them. As a result, there is more and more smuggling, and at the same time, Chaozhou and Shantou taxes are very heavy, making it impossible for legitimate merchants to compete with smuggled goods, creating opportunities for smugglers. Moreover, their smuggled goods are mostly transported to the Datong Ice Factory at the end of Shen Zhao Road at night for wholesale storage, and the inspectors do not intervene. This is another reason for the forced construction of the pier. (7th)

Commercial Depression in Tianjin

Most Bankruptcies in the Silver and Money Industry

Tianjin Correspondence: Since last spring, the commercial sector in Tianjin has experienced abnormal development, with a world of difference between the business conditions of stores in the concessions and those outside the concessions. The major department stores have either moved into the concessions or reduced their scope and established branches in the concessions. The once most prosperous Dongmalu, Beidaguan, and Houjiahou streets have almost no second- or third-class stores left, except for a few sixth- or seventh-class stores. Houjiahou's used clothing street, the concentration area of large stores, became desolate after last spring, with each store seeing few customers and hardly any customers all day long. Those stores with more than 200 years of history, which used to maintain their facade with wholesale dealers, were also directly affected by the extreme economic hardship and commercial depression in the outer counties and towns. Zhugang Alley, the main area for cotton yarn, was also unable to support itself due to the influence of cotton yarn dealers in the concessions. From the Jintang Bridge north to the new train station on Dajing Road, a street five miles long, there are no large stores. Those with slightly thicker capital have all moved into the concessions. In and around the past year, each store has prominently displayed reduced prices for clearance sales, or directly wrote [Year-end Sale at Cost], even pharmacies have used discounts of 20% or 12.5% to attract customers, but the effect of attracting customers is still very small. Therefore, many stores have closed down, especially in the silver and money industry, where many were unable to recover loans on time, causing a lot of trouble, and more went bankrupt. Stores in the concessions seem to be prosperous on the surface, but in fact, due to the heavy taxes, they often cannot make ends meet. Each store has no choice but to embrace the principle of small profits, selling outwards as long as they do not lose money. Therefore, although each store is crowded with customers, in reality, they are all strong on the outside but empty on the inside, and their plight is no less than that of those outside the concessions. Among the British, French, Italian, and Japanese concessions in Tianjin, the more prosperous ones are the Lixian in the French concession and Route 26, as well as the Asahi Street in the Japanese concession. However, the Japanese concession has repeatedly experienced disturbances, and due to the unstable situation in North China, those with any status are wary and hesitant to move forward, so the stores have also been affected. The stores in the French concession's Lixian are all located at the junction of Han and Japanese, and have become the commercial center of the whole Tianjin port. According to a survey by the Social Affairs Bureau, there were about 32,000 stores with a business tax of 14th grade or above outside the concessions in the year before last. Last year, the number of bankruptcies followed one after another, and now there are only more than 21,000 left. The number of stores in the concessions is also estimated to be more than 20,000. Although there have been continuous increases last year, most of them moved from Chinese streets, and there are not many newly opened ones. Although the period for the year-end closing of accounts has passed, it cannot yet be regarded as without any changes. It is feared that after the Lantern Festival, there will still be stores closing down inside and outside the concessions. (7th)

8th Division Recovers Bandit Area of Ning Le

Captures Pseudo-Central Committee Member Lou Mengxia, etc.

And Seizes Over 600 Long and Short Guns

Gan News: Since being ordered to suppress the remaining bandits between Ningdu and Lean, the 8th Division has spared no effort. Bandit nests in Luokou, Zhangguan, Xiaotian of Ningdu, and Yinshui, Dajinzhu, Zhongcun, etc. of Lean have all been successively recovered. Approximately 3,000-4,000 gun-wielding bandits, including the two independent regiments under the jurisdiction of the pseudo-Jiangxi Military Region, independent battalions of various counties, guerrilla units, advance teams, the pseudo-Jiangxi Provincial Government Guards, and the pseudo-Security Bureau, have been wiped out. In particular, in a battle near Zhongcun, the Liu Zhenshe Regiment of the 8th Division's Li Ying Brigade was especially valiant. In addition to killing many bandits on the spot, it successively captured pseudo-Central Executive Committee member and concurrently Director of the Jiangxi Security Bureau, Lou Mengxia (pseudo-Executive Minister Huo Tongguang committed suicide and his head has been severed), pseudo-Jiangxi Provincial Committee member Xiahou Yong, pseudo-Military Region Sabotage Minister Luo Chunmei, and more than 800 male and female bandits. They seized more than 500 rifles, 18 heavy machine guns, more than 20 submachine guns, more than 30 Mauser pistols, one silver seal of the pseudo-Jiangxi Provincial Government, manufacturing machines, lithographic printing machines, and multiple sewing machines. The remaining bandits in the area have been completely suppressed. Residents who had sought refuge elsewhere are all leading the old and carrying the young, returning to their homes that they had left several years ago.

Songjiang

Songjiang Branch of the Red Cross Society

Adds a Refugee Shelter

The Songjiang branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society established a Zhejiang drought refugee shelter. Due to the surge in the number of refugees being accommodated, they plan to borrow the Minglun Hall of the Confucius Temple to set up a second shelter. They have telegraphed the headquarters of the Chinese Red Cross Society for the record. Here is the reply telegram: "To the Songjiang Branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society, Vegetables [蔬] for Jian [鑒], Fish [魚] for telegram understood. The report of the proposed addition of a second shelter, borrowing the Minglun Hall of the Confucius Temple to expand accommodation, shows great enthusiasm for relief. Approval for the record is granted. It is still hoped that it will be handled with care. Seal of the Chinese Red Cross Society." It is also heard that Geng Junji, a Songjiang gentleman and currently a secretary of the Shanghai Municipal Government, deeply appreciates the branch's handling of the Zhejiang refugee shelter this time and has joined the Red Cross Society as a full member. In addition to household expenses, he donates all the rent rice he collects to the shelter to benefit the refugees. He also plans to gather like-minded people to thoroughly repair the Minglun Hall of the Confucius Temple after the shelter is closed. He also intends to find ways to ensure that the Songjiang branch's funds are permanently available. It is noted that Mr. Geng has always enthusiastically promoted local public welfare undertakings, so the people of Songjiang admire him endlessly.

Extension of the Art Exhibition

The Painting and Calligraphy Exhibition jointly organized by the Changqiao Elementary School of Songjiang County and the Songfeng Painting and Calligraphy Society at the Xin Songjiang Society on Songwei Road since the Lunar New Year has gathered hundreds of masterpieces by famous painters and calligraphers from home and abroad. The exhibits are dazzling and beautiful beyond compare. It has been open for more than a week, and visitors have been flocking to it, with over a thousand people daily. There has also been enthusiastic purchasing of paintings and calligraphy. It is learned that many people from other places who purchased painting and calligraphy vouchers issued by the society in advance have been unable to come to the exhibition to collect their items due to the continuous rain in recent days, and have sent letters requesting an extension of the closing date. Therefore, the organizers of the society, to avoid disappointing art lovers, have decided to extend the exhibition until February 18th (the Lantern Festival on the Lunar Calendar). It is also learned that the pricing department of the society has new works arriving, such as landscapes by Ms. Yu Yinzhan, running script by Ms. Yu Luxue, the eight-part script and running script by the Liu sisters, daughters of Mr. Liu San, Liu Xiu and Liu [𦇢], landscapes and flowers by the couple Liu Zhixun and Yu Yunfang, and mountain flowers and plants by the Sang Bo Yi and Zhong Ming brothers. Those who wish to order should act quickly, lest they miss the opportunity.

Suzhou

High Court Moves to Zhenjiang, Sets Up Branch Court

The Jiangsu High Court, currently located on Daoqian Street in Suzhou, is reportedly being moved to Zhenjiang by a decision of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and preparations are actively underway. It is expected to be implemented around July or August this year. Another Jiangsu High Court Fifth Branch will be established in Suzhou to handle appeals from Wu County, Kunshan, Wujiang, Qingpu, Changshu, Wuxi, and other counties. The address will be the original site of the Jiangsu High Court. The local Lawyers Association specifically raised the issue of the High Court's move to Zhenjiang for study at yesterday's review meeting. They unanimously advocated postponing the move to Zhenjiang and appointed Lu Hongyi to draft a memorial. Other legal organizations will also make statements on this matter.

Wuxi

The Puzzling Case of Forced Enlistment

There is a new recruit transportation station located in the Sanguan Hall of Chong'an Temple in this city. The person in charge is Wang Xiaoxian (nicknamed Wang Datou). Outsiders are mostly unclear about its operation. On weekdays, he constantly lures ignorant people inside and detains them. The other day, Tang Laoting from Piaoyang, Ren Laowu, Hu Baosheng, Zhang Jinying, etc. from Yixing took advantage of the Lunar New Year to come to Wuxi to perform lion dances, hoping to earn a small profit. Unexpectedly, when passing in front of the Sanguan Hall, Zhao Laosan, a cook from the station, told Tang and the others that the station currently needed several cooks, with a monthly salary of 16 yuan. Why not give up the lion dance life and take it? When Tang and the others refused, Zhao used his skills and flowery words to forcibly drag Tang and the other four inside and detain them. Until last night, Zhu, the wife of Ren Laowu, searched everywhere because her husband had not returned and only learned that he had entered the military. She rushed to the Sanguan Hall to seek a meeting with her husband and persuade him to return home. However, she was blocked by the recruitment office there and not allowed to meet him. Zhu, helpless, burst into tears, extremely miserable. At that time, Hang Tianliang, an employee of the First District Office, happened to see it, inquired about the details, and reported it to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau on her behalf. The police dispatched officers to summon Wang Xiaoxian, his assistant Lu Luogao, and Yang Laoting, Ren Laowu, Hu Baosheng, Zhang Jinying, etc. to the bureau. After questioning by Bureau Member Fan in court, it was stated that Jiangnan counties had long banned recruitment, and Wang and others clearly had fraudulent behavior. They were ordered to be temporarily detained in the bureau, pending instructions from the General Bureau for verification.

A Retrospective of Last Year's Commerce

Wuxi has always been known for its prosperous commerce among the counties in the interior of Jiangsu Province. However, since the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, it has been affected by the depression. The silk cocoon industry has declined severely, the rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, and the market is extremely bleak. During this winding-up period, although all industries were able to weather the difficulties, they were stretched thin. This year, businesses unanimously advocated tightening their belts. The situation of each industry is summarized below to measure the rise and fall of commerce. (1) Banking Industry: Shanghai banks regard Wuxi as a region for using funds, so they have come to Wuxi to open branches one after another. There are currently ten banks, including the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Shanghai Bank, the Jiangsu Farmers Bank, the Continental Bank, the China Industrial Bank, the Xingye Bank, and the Zhongnan Commercial Bank. In addition to operating remittances and mortgages, they also provide credit to shops, so their businesses are extremely developed. In the first half of last year, each bank had excess cash and competed to lend at low interest rates, with weekly interest rates dropping to below 7%. By October, they received a notice from the head office to stop lending, and interest rates gradually rose, rising to over 1%. At the end of the year, each bank had a slight surplus, with the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications having the most, each with a surplus of 10,000 to 20,000 yuan. The rest were average. (2) Money Shops: After the failure of the silk factories, they all suffered losses in conjunction. The number decreased from 18 to 9. Furthermore, affected by the competition from banks, it became increasingly difficult for their business to develop. Fortunately, they proceeded cautiously, so they were still able to make a small profit at the end of the year. The Fuyu and Yonghengfeng money shops each made a surplus of 10,000 yuan. The rest, such as Fuyuan, Ruichang, Run Shen, Yuyuan, and Fengyi, also had slight surpluses. Others, such as Yunyu, Fuchang, and Sheng, were just enough to cover expenses. However, the Yunyu money shop is not listed because the shareholders have no intention of operating it. (3) Cotton Mills: In the midst of this extreme depression, each factory paid attention to internal reforms, so their products became more refined. Last year's business was the best for Lixin, with a surplus of more than 100,000 yuan. Qingfeng and Shenxin also each had a surplus of tens of thousands of yuan. The next best, such as Guangqin, Zhenxin, Yukang, and Yeqin, could only cover expenses because their cotton yarn could not compare. (4) Wheat Flour Factories: The industry refused foreign wheat last year. Although the raw materials were slightly insufficient, they reduced production, allowing the market price to be averaged. During the summer, the price of flour gradually rose, and sales became smooth again. Each factory rushed to manufacture, but it was still not enough to sell. However, once past August, the market repeated its silence. Each factory's surplus was 150,000 yuan for Jiufeng and a total of 200,000 yuan for Maoxin 1 and 2 factories, and more than 70,000 yuan for Tailong. (5) Silk and Cloth Industry: Since the January 28th Incident, followed by the failure of the silk factories and the decline of the rural economy, the industry has been greatly affected. Therefore, they closed down one after another, from more than 50 to 38. Last year, those in the rotten industry united and reorganized industry regulations, so they were able to make a profit at the end of the year. Rixin, Shihe, and Shitaisheng were the best. In addition, Maolun, Jiuyu, Jiulun, and Tianlun were all able to cover expenses. The rest were average. (6) Dried Goods Industry: There are 26 major firms that have joined the industry association. Last year, affected by the drought and the market decline, business was only about 70% of the previous year. Wanda was the best, with a surplus of about 7,000 to 8,000 yuan. The rest were difficult to profit from. Taoyao Yanhe Zhi Ruhao, a shop with more than 20 years of history, closed down during the winding-up period due to poor business and is currently being liquidated.

Towns and Villages Robbed During the Lunar New Year

During the Lunar New Year, gambling is rampant in various villages and towns as usual, making it easy for thieves to hide. Song Zhongyang, a national doctor in the Langangqiao Town in the west countryside, has a thriving business. His son, Song Chushi, is currently the principal of Shuqin Girls' High School. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 9th, four thieves suddenly broke into the Song family's house. At the time, Song happened to be out visiting patients, and only the housewife and two servants were left at home, who were all tied up. After being robbed for about an hour, they packed up the soft goods and gold jewelry and left, with a loss of about 1,500 yuan.

Preparations for Dredging Huangtian Port are Underway

The issue of dredging Huangtian Port in this city has been repeatedly discussed and planned. The dredging has been approved by the Construction Department, with a budget of 160,000 yuan. The province provided 65,000 yuan, and the remaining 95,000 yuan will be drawn from the local construction fee item. The engineering office is attached to the Zhenwu Canal Dredging Engineering Office and is named [Zhenwu Canal Dredging Engineering No. 9 Section Office of Huangtian Port.] It is temporarily borrowing a portion of the County Party Headquarters' building for office space. The position of section chief is concurrently held by Lu Bingzhang, the section chief of the County Government's Third Section. One engineer and two engineering staff have not yet been determined. As for the dam construction and dredging machines, personnel have been dispatched to negotiate. On the 10th, the County Government convened a discussion meeting to discuss all the progress matters.

Director Yu Pays Attention to the Huangcao Bridge Homicide Case

Su [蘇] Provincial Civil Affairs Director Yu Jingtang recently learned from newspaper reports about the homicide case in Caoqiao Town in the Eighth District. Considering that it involved the killing of a person by the security team and that the circumstances were seriously suspicious, he specifically instructed Police Inspector Li Kaizhou to conduct an investigation when he departed for inspections in various counties. After arriving in Changzhou on the 9th, Inspector Li went to the County Government to meet with Secretary Yang Zhaoyun and inquired about the circumstances of the Caoqiao case. Secretary Yang replied that the County Government only had reports from the District Office, etc., and that the case was currently under investigation by the court's procuratorate and had not yet been clarified. Li then accompanied Yang to the court to meet with Chief Prosecutor Yang Kongyi and inquired in great detail. On the morning of the 10th, Li had not yet obtained the key points. Whether the security team leader Zhou Zhongsheng had any adulterous vendetta or if it was the accidental killing of a thief still needed further investigation. In addition to going to the County Government to review the case files, he also inquired about the basis of the newspaper reports. He then learned that the case was first disclosed by the Wuxi National Herald. Li then took a car to Wuxi in the afternoon to investigate before returning to the office to report.
