Bank Inspection Report Compilation

Central Bank's 223rd Issuance Reserve Inspection Report states: In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Act, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the issuance of convertible banknotes by this bank. The 223rd inspection was held on February 9th, 1935 at the Issuance Department of this bank. The inspection results are hereby announced as follows: (A) The total amount of silver dollar convertible banknotes issued is 90,388,051 silver dollars, including 83,838,200 silver dollar notes and 6,549,851 fractional currency notes. The total amount of convertible banknote reserves is 90,388,051 silver dollars, including 71,288,051 silver dollars in cash reserves. This cash reserve is stored in the following locations: 67,347,012 silver dollars in the bank's issuance vault, 2,117,154 silver dollars in branches in various ports, and 1,823,885 silver dollars deposited with other banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 19,100,000 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible banknotes issued is 373,324.70 yuan. The total amount of customs gold convertible banknote reserves is 373,324.70 yuan. This reserve includes 7,351 taels, 9 mace and 5 fen of standard gold, valued at 50,779, which is equivalent to 373,324.70 customs gold yuan. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve should be 60% and the guarantee reserve should be 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is consistent with the regulations. This report is hereby issued. February 11th, 1935. Li Fuxun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Supervisor Xie Mingdong, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Ji.

China Industrial Bank's 42nd Issuance Department Reserve Report states: The China Industrial Bank's Issuance Department's reserves are completely separate from the business department's funds, and the reserves are fully adequate. The number of issuance reserves on February 9th, 1935, is announced as follows: The total amount of convertible banknotes issued is 33,891,013 yuan, including 18,400,613 yuan issued by this bank, 7,474,400 yuan issued by affiliated banks, and 8,010,000 yuan used by banks and firms. Except for the portion used by various banks and firms, which is inspected according to the original method, the amount of convertible banknotes issued by this affiliated bank for this inspection is 25,881,013 yuan. The amount of convertible banknote reserves of this affiliated bank is 25,881,013 yuan, including 16,126,017.27 yuan in cash reserves and 9,754,995.73 yuan in guarantee reserves. The above two items, the cash reserve accounting for more than 60% and the guarantee reserve accounting for less than 40%, have been checked without error. Accountant Zhang Yiyan.

The Four Banks Reserve Treasury is jointly established by the Y盐业 (Salt Industry), 金城 (Jincheng), 中南 (Zhongnan), and 大陆 (Dalu) banks, and is specifically responsible for issuing banknotes for the Zhongnan Bank. According to the treasury's issuance regulations, the banknotes are issued with full reserves, with a cash reserve of at least 60% and a guarantee reserve of at most 40%. A public announcement is made once a week, and it is audited by the auditors of the four banks and accountants. The Xujiahui Observatory's weather report at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong and its surrounding areas were clear, cold, and had strong northwesterly winds. Special Feature

Two Lines of Approach to Japan (Continued) Lin Bosheng

...After Reading Xu Daolin's [A Review of Sino-Japanese Relations]...

Finally, let me add a few words.

In one passage, Xu Wen mentions the opinion paper published by Chiang Kai-shek in January 1932, in which his diplomatic stance towards Japan was summarized in twelve characters: [No severance of relations, no declaration of war, no peace talks, no treaty signing]. Mr. Xu believes that although it is [not thorough], it [cannot be denied that this policy is a relatively unfeasible method, because countries with vastly unequal national power and military strength can only use this policy and strategy to deal with each other]. I believe that the eight characters [Negotiate on one hand, resist on the other] proposed by Wang Jingwei after the September 18th Incident also convey the same meaning. At the time, he advocated resisting on one hand because he saw that the Northeast garrison did not resist, and he advocated negotiating on one hand because he saw that the whole country advocated not negotiating. Compared side by side, there is no difference. The only difference is that [No severance of relations, no declaration of war, no peace talks, no treaty signing] establishes the scope of diplomatic and military policy from a passive perspective, while [Negotiate on one hand, resist on the other] points out the direction of diplomatic and military policy from a positive perspective. Why is it said to be a method among unfeasible methods? Because with this approach, no one dares to say that they have any certainty of success, but in fact, it has to be done arduously.

After the January 28th Incident, under the leadership of Wang Jingwei and Zhuang Wenjie, the political and military authorities, China has been following this path completely.

The meaning of negotiation and resistance has been mentioned above. Negotiation means seeking a solution under extreme tolerance, and resistance means that when tolerance is no longer possible and concessions cannot be made, for the sake of territorial sovereignty and the lives and property of the people, we must rise up for legitimate defense. During the Songhu War, Japan used force, which had reached the point where tolerance was no longer possible and concessions could not be made, so we tried our best to resist. After the resistance failed, we were responsible for negotiating and signing the Songhu Armistice Agreement. This is the process of negotiation and resistance. During the North China War, Japan used force again; it had also reached the point where tolerance was no longer possible and concessions could not be made; so we tried our best to resist. After the resistance failed, we were responsible for negotiating and signing the Tanggu Truce. This is also the process of negotiation and resistance. As for appealing to the League of Nations, the arrival of the League of Nations Investigation Team in China, the drafting of the Lytton Report, and the League of Nations resolution recognizing Japan as an aggressor and the puppet organization as a puppet, all of which gave China a fair sympathy, were also part of the negotiation process. Naturally, land was lost due to non-resistance in the past, and land is now lost due to resistance. Since negotiation is necessary anyway, it seems that there was no need to resist in the first place. Since we resisted, it seems that we should not have negotiated later. Looking back on the matter, we cannot say that this approach is thorough, but considering the circumstances of the day, we cannot deny that this approach was forced by circumstances. With the current national strength, resistance will inevitably fail, who doesn't know this? Knowing it and still resisting is precisely a firm expression of fighting for the country's personality and seeking the nation's survival. Success or failure is not its purpose. It is known that resistance and negotiation seem to be contradictory, but in fact, they are complementary. Resistance leads to negotiation, and the more effective the resistance, the more hopeful the negotiation. As for the resistance, there is no follow-up internally and no foreign aid externally. In the end, negotiation is known to be out of desperation. On January 23rd last year, Mr. Wang made a political report at the fourth plenary session of the fourth session of the Central Executive Committee, in which he made an analogy. He said, what should be the first step if a village encounters bandits who break into the gate in the middle of the night? Naturally, it is to hold the second gate firmly, and the second step is to beat the gong to call for help. When the gong rings and reinforcements do not arrive, and the gate has been lost, and it seems that even the second gate cannot be defended, what should be done at that time? In order to defend the second gate, it is necessary to stop the gong and plan how to strengthen the defense inside the second gate and how to ease the attack outside the second gate. From the Songhu Armistice Agreement to the Tanggu Truce, the situation is exactly like this. Until today, the situation in China is still like this.

From this, it can be seen that for the past three years, China has been following the second path I mentioned above.

During these three years, China's national lifeline has gone through countless crises, the people of the whole country have suffered countless sacrifices, and the government authorities have tasted countless hardships before reaching today.

After today, will China continue to adhere to the Wang-Chiang line that has remained unchanged for the past three years? Or will there be other paths?

V

As I was writing this, I just received Tokyo dispatches from the Associated Press and Reuters, which said that the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun published a long article by the newspaper's political correspondent on January 29, stating the fundamental principles of Japan's policy toward China. It is expected that the Japanese government will use these principles as the basis, hoping that China will abandon its old traditional policy of attacking and making friends from afar, and said that the Chinese Ministry of Foreign Affairs will pay attention to the following points to determine its new policy toward China:

(1) Maintain the integrity of China's territory, hoping that the first step is to suppress the communist bandits and sweep away all anti-foreign movements.

(2) Formal negotiations to restore normal relations between China and Japan.

(3) The Japanese government will continue not to interfere in China's internal affairs and will remain neutral in China's party struggles, but if there is one person in China who is willing and able to assume full responsibility for governing China, Japan is prepared to expand its political, military, economic and other assistance to him.

(4) Japan is willing to exchange ambassadors with China and conclude a Sino-Japanese agreement in accordance with the Japan-[Manchukuo] agreement, but China must realize that China and Japan are interdependent and recognize the importance of their position in the peace of the Far East, and not rely solely on Europe and the United States. (5) Japan is willing to conclude another agreement with China on Far Eastern political issues, because Japan no longer recognizes the principle of multilateral conventions such as the Nine-Power Treaty that allows third parties to participate. (6) Regarding Far Eastern military issues, Japan hopes that China will promise not to seek assistance from the League of Nations again, and it is not impossible to withdraw from the League of Nations, and to replace European and American advisors with Japanese advisors.

(7) Japan believes that the organization of a Sino-[Manchukuo]-Japanese group is an extremely important move, and Japan is prepared to provide China with expanded financial assistance for this.

(8) If China can express its sincerity regarding the above points, Japan is prepared to change the North China Armistice Agreement into a permanent treaty and establish a neutral zone between China and [Manchukuo]. (9) Japan believes that negotiations on a possible Sino-Japanese treaty should begin six months after March 27, when Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations will take effect.

Comparing this record with Foreign Minister Hirota's recent speech in the Japanese parliament, it is not difficult to see what the meaning of Japan's so-called change in policy toward China is. It seems necessary to add a few words to the Japanese.

If Japan truly has the sincerity to abandon military aggression, open up a new Sino-Japanese situation, and restore normal diplomatic relations, it will have only benefits and no harm to Japan itself, to East Asian peace, and even to world peace. I believe that the Chinese side should also not be indecisive and should consider it in accordance with established policies. The reasons are as follows:

First, in terms of the international situation, from the agreement between France and Italy at the beginning of this year, through the Saar plebiscite to the recent visit of Austrian Prime Minister Goering to Poland and the joint declaration of Britain and France, a series of international events reflect the international crisis everywhere, reflect the life of anxiety that European countries are living under so-called armed peace, and at the same time show the psychology of European countries' people's aversion to war everywhere. Show the painstaking efforts and efforts of European governments to avoid war (or at least delay war) and maintain peace. The European situation can be said to have a temporary possibility of peace. What is most threatening to world peace is East Asia, and what is most threatening to East Asian peace is Japan. If we add it up, Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations will be completed in March of this year, and the Washington Nine-Power Treaty and the Naval Agreement have already been notified of their abolition in December of last year, then we can understand that today's Japan is taking a dead end that threatens world peace (Note). It is exactly the so-called crucial moment to start a war, and it is also the moment to maintain peace. It is also the so-called rein in at the edge of the cliff. The Japanese people, from the poor masses to the important ministers, scholars, elders, and soldiers, should all be calm and think carefully at this time for the ultimate interests of Japan, for the peace of East Asia, and for world peace. This is one.

Secondly, in terms of Sino-Japanese relations, there is no need to mention those words about being of the same race and the same culture. Just from an economic point of view, Japan is an advanced industrial country, and China is a vast agricultural country. Japan is an island country, and China is a continental country. Under the principle of international division of labor, the economic relations between China and Japan cannot be separated or divided. It must be known that military aggression and political control are the methods used by militarists in the 18th and 19th centuries. This era has passed. The division of labor and connection between countries is the inevitable result of the development of world economic activities, especially the inevitable process of group economies. Under this trend, all deformed combinations will inevitably disintegrate and be replaced by equal and naturally developed division of labor and connections. As a method, the result must be a loss outweighs the gains. Just calculate the strength spent in occupying the Northeast and the conflict between colonial capital and imperial capital created in the Northeast in the past two or three years to understand. On the Chinese side, it should also be known that although the division of labor and connection between countries and economic aggression are very similar, they are not completely indistinguishable. We cannot say that before China has achieved an equal status and a considerable national strength, a Japanese yen, a British pound, or a US dollar in China will not contain the meaning of aggression, but we cannot say that a British pound invades the United States when it arrives in New York, or a US dollar invades Britain when it arrives in London. This statement seems ridiculous, but it can also be seen that the relationship between countries is like differential and integral calculus, the more divided, the more subtle, the closer the integration, the complex, and it is by no means a simple printed arithmetic formula of addition, subtraction, multiplication, and division that can be solved. The so-called equal status and the so-called national strength cannot be achieved overnight, nor can they be estimated by simply comparing that one thing. It all depends on the development of the situation to make a judgment. Therefore, I personally believe that under this principle, there is a possibility and necessity to consider the economic relations between China and Japan. This is two.

What should be paid attention to here:

First, as for the so-called formal negotiations to restore normal relations between China and Japan, if the Japanese side is indeed sincere, the Chinese government should be open and honest based on the established policy, without so-called abandoning policies or changing directions.

Second, non-recognition of the puppet Manchukuo is an iron rule that the Chinese government and people unanimously abide by. There is no room for negotiation at all for those who violate this iron rule or are suspected of factually or formally recognizing the puppet state.

Third, under the principle of freedom and equality, the Chinese government can give appropriate consideration to the economic relations between China and Japan, but this consideration is entirely based on the economic and geographical relations between China and Japan. The so-called Sino-"Manchukuo"-Japanese group can be said to be the most ridiculous.

Fourth, the so-called consideration of economic relations between the two countries is based on the principle of freedom and equality, which absolutely cannot contain any exclusive or exclusive nature. Under the same principle, China has its own economic relations with European and American countries. In other words, China must still adhere to the established policy of not uniting with Europe and the United States to exclude Japan, nor uniting with Japan to exclude Europe and the United States.

Fifth, the so-called consideration of economic relations between the two countries clearly means economy, which absolutely cannot be attached to any political or military conditions. The Osaka Mainichi Shimbun claimed that if there is one person in China who is willing and able to assume full responsibility for governing China, Japan is prepared to expand its political, economic, military and other assistance to him. This is completely the biggest mistake in Japan's traditional thinking toward China. I dare to tell the Japanese that China under the rule of the Kuomintang will never have Yuan Shikai first, to sign the 21 Articles in disguise, and China will never be the second Korea, to sign the so-called "annexation of Korea" agreement in disguise. Japan does not need to entice us with this again. If China needs the assistance of Japan, no matter in which aspect, it must be due to China's autonomy, and secondly, it must be based on the needs of the Chinese people.

In other words, it is very good if Japan has the sincerity to break the deadlock between China and Japan, but judging from the records of the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, the traditional mistakes and ideas of the Japanese have not been eliminated, which is a great regret. February 1, 1935, in Shanghai.

Chunqiu

Drips

— (Chen Yunsu)

The literature we need now is the bread that can fill our bellies, not luxuries solely for decoration.

The god of happiness will not descend on people's heads out of thin air, so those who buy lottery tickets and prize coupons are the biggest fools in the world.

In the past, people often looked at the goods before discussing the price, and cast the net before counting the fish; now, people set the table before discussing the goods, and count the fish before casting the net.

Modern society is like a kaleidoscope, from the mansions of the rich and powerful to the slums of the poor; from the stench of wine and meat in the vermilion gates to the frozen bones on the road; from scientific foreign PhDs and masters to theocratic monks and nuns, everything is available.

Lost Husband and Finger

— Wang Yun

The gambling atmosphere in Xinhui is very strong, with gambling dens of all sizes spread throughout the cities and villages. Especially in these first few days of the year, those with a Liu Panlong addiction are already itching to try, regardless of whether they will lose their homes, they all go to the gambling dens to satisfy their gambling cravings.

A farmer named Zhang from the countryside is a loyal believer of the gambling god Bodhisattva, losing more as he gambles, and gambling more as he loses, with the appearance of "not giving up until reaching the Yellow River." His wife, Wu, repeatedly pleaded bitterly, shedding tears, but he treated his wife's words as wind passing by his ears. As soon as he heard there was a gambling den somewhere, he eagerly rushed to gamble, not hesitating to pawn clothes and belongings to pay homage to his gambling expenses.

One day, he took more than three yuan of gambling money to the Shalu Market gambling den to gamble. By the end of the gambling session, not only was his pocket empty, but he also owed more than ten yuan in bad debts. He had no way to pay it off. The gamblers were in an uproar and imprisoned Zhang in a dark room, inflicting severe beatings on him. Zhang, unable to bear the pain, begged to pay it off within three days and asked a familiar gambling friend to guarantee it before he was released and returned home.

Two days later, Zhang invited his wife to go to Xiaogang Market to shop. Wu did not suspect anything and went with a basket. Who knew that as soon as they arrived at Xiaogang Market, someone detained Wu and showed her her husband's note, only then did she realize that her husband had sold Wu to Li of Xiaogang as a concubine for a price of thirty yuan to repay his gambling debts.

Zhang obtained the money from the sale and went to Shalu Market, wanting to try his luck again after repaying his debts. Who knew that his luck was not good, and he lost every battle. The money in his pocket became "empty again." After returning home, he was unusually depressed. He accidentally looked up and saw Wu's photo still hanging on the wall—he thought that the small portrait was still there, but the person had already become a commodity. At that moment, grief arose from within, and his spirit suffered a major shock. He rushed into the kitchen and cut off his index finger with a kitchen knife. Blood flowed like a stream, and he fainted. Neighbors found out and, after waking him up, sent him to the hospital. Isn't the outcome of a gambler losing his wife and finger?

Talking About Banknotes

— Zhu Ying

"Black eyes seeing silver," this saying is outdated now, because snow-white silver dollars are rarely circulating in the current market. Nine out of ten things that come from the east hand to the west hand are colorful banknotes.

Hygienists say that "banknotes" are the easiest things to spread infectious diseases, because when banknotes pass through the hands of those with infectious diseases, bacteria will attach to the banknotes and be transmitted to those without infectious diseases through the medium of banknotes. But even though that's what they say, I have never seen any hygienist refuse to accept unsterilized banknotes. And at the same time, I have never found any banknotes discarded by hygienists on the street.

I have a friend who has a special interest in banknotes. Every banknote that passes through his hands has a small stamp or signature on the corner. He is a salaried worker with a monthly income of a little over one hundred yuan, but according to him, after stamping and signing for three years, only one ten-yuan note and three five-yuan notes have passed through his hands a second time. The rest, once used, have never been seen again.

In the interior, in places where transportation is not very convenient, there is still a habit of using only ×× bank notes and refusing to use other bank notes, even though other banks are as reliable as ×× bank in Shanghai, but in the interior, it is somewhat different. This is just like the "foreign bank notes are most popular" that used to be popular in Shanghai, which is equally incomprehensible.

Miss Tang

— Wang Xikeng

Anyone who knows Miss Tang must admit that she is a stunner, a lovely person.

Miss Tang is slender, not too tall, not too short, with a well-proportioned figure, wearing a well-fitting fashion, walking gracefully with small steps, showing that she is a complete modern woman; and even more so, she has a slightly yellowish and peach-colored oval face, dark hair, trimmed moth eyebrows, moist and bright autumn waves, and thin red lips, which is truly very beautiful, very beautiful.

And that's not all. Miss Tang also has a special advantage; that is, she treats people very kindly, always smiling before speaking, and showing goodwill to everyone. Originally, Miss Tang's beautiful appearance was already very moving; what's more, on those tender and rosy cheeks, there are two shallow dimples, and her thin red lips are slightly upturned, revealing two rows of neat jade teeth, what a soul-stirring smiling face.

Really, anyone who has experienced Miss Tang's smile feels that this smile is subtle, charming, and contains infinite depth and mystery. However, it is also in her shallow dimples that I don't know how many young people have been intoxicated and how many patriots have been turned upside down!

But then again, although Miss Tang's actions are so gentle and her expression is so kind, she also has times when she dislikes people. Because, to say nothing else, if you speak bluntly and don't suit her, she will wrinkle her eyebrows and scold you in a delicate and coquettish voice, "You dead Jiangbei old man."

World News

Dog Obsession and Dogs

— Huang Yingdai

The Mystery of Women's Love for Dogs

In European and American countries, almost every woman in every family has more than one pet dog. These women may have servants all over the house and are usually unwilling to do any housework themselves, but they personally take care of the dog's food, bathing, etc. Their love for dogs is greater than their love for their husbands. When they are in the mood, they hug their beloved dogs and give them a few kisses. Moreover, the habit of kissing dogs is more common among women than men. Those young girls are unwilling to kiss men casually, but they are happy to kiss the dogs they keep without stopping. Isn't this a riddle that we can't figure out?

Kissing Dogs Spreads Swelling Disease

A doctor in the Westminster district of England once discovered a woman who died from kissing dogs often. This woman had a habit of always kissing her dogs non-stop when she fed them. As a result, she fell ill and could not be saved. The doctor at the Red Cross Hospital, after examining her with X-rays, found that she had a hydatid cyst in her abdomen. This cyst is formed by the eggs of small worms from the dog's body entering the human body. Therefore, it proves that she contracted this germ because she often kissed dogs. Moreover, there are many dog owners who have hydatid cysts in their abdomens from kissing dogs!

Dog Owner Arrested Because of Dog

Once, a person committed a crime. He was a dog lover, and the dog he kept was almost inseparable from him every day. One day, he and another friend were sitting next to the stove, and his dog was also with them. The detectives arrived, but the detectives only knew that he had a dog and did not recognize him. It was impossible to prove which of the two was the criminal at the time. The clever detective thought for a moment and came up with a plan. He went over and deliberately kicked the dog. The dog owner, seeing his beloved dog being kicked, immediately stood up to reason with the person. However, the detective immediately pulled out a pistol and captured the wanted criminal.

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 8: Remote Place, Light Official, Distant Strong Commander; Hua Hall, Grand Banquet, Outside, a Pitiful Worm

Among them, the one with the loudest laughter was County Magistrate Zhou Yourong. I only heard him say loudly: Since I am not an official that the imperial court cherishes very much, then I will not accept the insignificant reputation of the local community. Hahaha! His face was facing the window, and just looking at the sweat dripping from his forehead, one could imagine his heroic feelings. In fact, it was not just him, all the people present had red faces. At this time, the dish being served was fried pork chops. This grand meal in Xi'an was originally no different from eating Chinese food in a Western style. The Western restaurant in Little Western Paradise did not prepare large plates for serving dishes, but rather increased the number of people to distribute the plates of pork chops to the guests, two plates at a time. Probably the pork chops were not fried very well, and the people eating them had to work hard to cut them, so the sound of knives and forks hitting the plates was very lively. Zhang Jiefu saw it from outside the window and thought to himself, eating Western food like this is really just showing off. Wherever there is such a show, Director Gao must be inside, but I don't know which one he is. As he was thinking this, he had to stretch his neck and look inside. Just at this moment, a gust of flying sand came down from the eaves, filling his neck with a lot of dust. He took two steps back and looked at the sky, but it was already dark and moonless, and the wind was whistling over his head. He also found it funny that a person from the East would never have seen people eating Western food, standing outside the window and forgetting everything. Isn't this a joke? Looking distantly into the glass window, the people eating the big meal were having a lively time. At the same time, a strange sound was heard in his ears. But this was not the sound of laughter, but the sound of sobbing, carried by the wind. There was a crying sound in this Little Western Paradise, which was naturally something to pay attention to, and he couldn't help but follow the sound. (131)

Misty Records of Royal Fragrance

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

For example, at this moment, Her Old Highness is discussing the affairs of Tongzhi with me. At this time, what she says can really be said to come from the bottom of her heart, and her attitude is even more infinitely solemn and earnest. Even if I spend my whole life atoning for my sins, kneeling under her feet without leaving for a moment, she will definitely not forgive me! In this way, doesn't she become a terrible madman? No, no, others may not be able to understand her true nature, but I have at least realized in my feelings the reason why her personality is so special, there is really a driving force; what is this driving force? This can be explained in two words, namely [pain].

Indeed, her position, her power, and all her material enjoyment can be said to be enough to make her happy, but how can her inner pain be remedied? Statistics show that her life is almost filled with all kinds of disappointments and hardships. When she was young, she was like a fresh flower about to bloom, very beautiful, very lively, and her heart was very satisfied to focus on Ronglu, but unexpectedly she was selected into the palace and became the concubine of Xianfeng, forcibly throwing her sweetheart aside, which was already very heartbreaking! Shen Bao Page Five

Education News: The Geng Indemnity Funds are Used to Launch New Educational Undertakings by the Ministry of Education

Forming a Committee with Various Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations to Implement

The Ministry of Education has Drafted Measures to Subsidize Volunteer Education, Vocational Education, and Establish National University Research Institutes

Nanjing Special Dispatch: According to reports, the third joint meeting of the Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations resolved to jointly launch new educational undertakings. Yesterday, according to the heads of the Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations, the content of this case differs slightly from the Beijing telegram reported on the 7th. The third joint meeting of the Geng Indemnity Fund resolved that the Sino-American, Sino-British, Sino-French, and Sino-Belgian Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations should jointly raise 1.1 million national currency annually, starting in the 24th year, for a period of three years, to launch the following educational undertakings: (1) 800,000 yuan will be used as subsidies to promote compulsory education. At the same time, the government should allocate a corresponding amount from the central financial budget for the 24th year as subsidies for compulsory education. (2) 150,000 yuan will be used to reward and assist vocational education throughout the country, and 150,000 yuan will be used to subsidize national universities in establishing research institutes. (3) The detailed measures for the above undertakings will be discussed and implemented by the Ministry of Education and the organizing committees of the various Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations in June of the 24th year. Before the establishment of the committee, the Ministry of Education will draft measures and notify the various Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations. Yesterday, the various Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations simultaneously received the three measures drafted by the Ministry of Education to promote compulsory education, vocational education, and establish university research institutes, requesting the various Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations to provide support, and stating that in the past, the funds from the Geng Indemnity Fund for educational and cultural undertakings were mostly used for higher education, while this time, except for a small part used for higher education, the majority will be used for compulsory education and vocational education. In the past, the Geng Indemnity Fund was mostly used to subsidize urban education undertakings in the interior, while this time, the subsidies will be extended to border education undertakings. As for the distribution of the burden of this fund among the four Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations of the United States, Britain, France, and Belgium, China and the United States will contribute 400,000 yuan, China and Britain 300,000 yuan, China and France 150,000 yuan, and China and Belgium 250,000 yuan, totaling 1.1 million yuan annually. The draft of the three measures proposed by the Ministry of Education is as follows:

(1) Outline of Measures to Subsidize the Promotion of Compulsory Education: From the 24th year to the 26th year, the Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations will allocate a total of 800,000 yuan annually as subsidies for compulsory education, in order to subsidize the government's promotion of compulsory education. Select one or two provinces from the remote provinces and select one or two cities from the municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan as the areas for the implementation of compulsory education with the aforementioned Geng Indemnity Fund subsidies. (2) Outline of Measures to Reward and Assist Vocational Education Throughout the Country: From the 20th year to the 26th year, the Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations will allocate a total of 150,000 yuan annually for rewarding and assisting vocational education. This subsidy will be limited to public or registered private vocational schools with excellent performance and meeting local needs. The number of schools receiving this subsidy should not be too large, in order to ensure that this subsidy can truly support a few model vocational schools. (3) Outline of Measures to Subsidize National Universities in Establishing Research Institutes: From the 24th year to the 26th year, the Geng Indemnity Fund Organizations will allocate a total of 150,000 yuan annually to subsidize two or three national universities in establishing research institutes. The universities receiving this subsidy will be designated after reference to the original proposal of the Ministry of Education.

General Evaluation Report of the National Labor Exhibition (4)

(G) Achievements in Sewing and Embroidery

1. General Evaluation

Generally speaking, the embroidery achievements from various provinces and cities are mostly exquisite, skillful, and lifelike. However, efforts should be made to make them popular, simple, and practical, so that the public has the ability to purchase and the opportunity to enjoy them. The manufacturing methods of sewing, weaving, white embroidery, and silk drawing are excellent, and the colors are beautiful, but there is very little expression in the cutting patterns for sewing. In the future, when learning to sew, more attention should be paid to cutting methods.

2. Detailed Evaluation

(1) Hangzhou Municipal Junior Girls' Vocational School of Home Economics and Commerce in Zhejiang Province has several oil painting embroideries with excellent needlework, color, and shadow lines, and the spirit of the characters is also good. The embroidery is completely done with fine threads, thin and dense, and very beautiful, and can only be made by those who have studied it thoroughly. In addition, there are also various sewing, weaving, and specimen picture frames, which can also be used for reference by those who study art.

(2) The random needle embroidery of Danyang Private Zhengze Girls' Vocational High School in Jiangsu Province is said to have been developed after more than ten years of research and is a different kind of needlework. The embroidered items are extremely exquisite, lifelike, and have elegant colors.

(3) The four cutting practice books of Nanjing Municipal Vocational Supplementary School contain very detailed cutting methods. Sewing in schools in various provinces pays attention to needlework but neglects cutting, because needlework is often easier than cutting. It should be known that learning to make clothes starts with sewing, but it is only considered complete after understanding the manufacturing method. Therefore, attention must be paid to cutting. The school's cutting practice book contains detailed clothing patterns and dimensions, showing that they usually pay great attention to cutting. The four cross-stitch embroideries of the Municipal No. 1 High School, although slightly rough, have a unique style with landscape colors like paintings. The embroidery method is also different from others, and other schools also use this embroidery method with commendable results.

(4) Shanghai Municipal Wuben Girls' High School exports a lot, among which the knitting method of children's woolen clothes is the most excellent, and the edging colors are also harmonious, with a lot of artistic significance.

(5) Qingdao has a large quantity and variety, among which the Municipal Girls' High School and Private Sheng Gong Girls' High School have better results.

(7) Fuzhou Vocational High School of Fujian Province has many kinds of embroidery, and the spirit, color, and light are also quite beautiful. Xiamen Vocational High School of Fujian Province has many sewing products, among which the girls' dress-like skirts and vest-like skirts have the most elegant colors and are also well-made, suitable for children. (8) The pinched cotton flower tiger of the Municipal No. 1 Girls' High School in Hankou, Hubei Province, has good spirit and color and has artistic value.

(9) Xiang embroidery has formed its own school in the embroidery world of our country and has been widely spread in recent years. At this exhibition, the female students of the province have the most achievements, and Xiang embroidery is especially characteristic. The embroidered portraits, landscapes, flowers, and calligraphy of famous artists are mostly delicate and lifelike and are quite commendable.

(10) Guangdong Private Guangdong Girls' Vocational School has a pair of cold embroidery picture frames, in which the flowers are made of down or cotton, with bright colors and lifelike leaves. The manufacturing method is simple and seems to be more labor-saving than embroidery, and it is also a novel aspect of artistic products.

(11) Chahar, Sichuan, Suiyuan, Qinghai, Ningxia, etc., do not have many excellent products in Chahar and Sichuan provinces. Suiyuan, Qinghai, and Ningxia have few products and their quality is inferior to other provinces.

Four. Evaluation of the Achievements of Labor Courses in Primary and Secondary Schools

1. General Evaluation

(1) In this exhibition, there are not many types and quantities of products needed in rural areas, but the majority of rural teachers and primary schools in Lu, Ji, and Cha provinces can pay attention to this. A small number of schools in other provinces and cities can also use local agricultural by-products such as cattails, yellow grass, rice straw, wheat straw, hemp skin, reeds, willows, and mountain hawthorn to weave baskets, boxes, bags, mats, mats, ropes, plain cloth, dustpans, brooms, shoes, shoes, accounts, and other applied objects. This kind of teaching material requires very simple equipment, and the raw materials can be collected locally. Teaching children and rural teachers and students with this material, in addition to the educational value of labor training, can also help the family. Therefore, it can be a suitable part of the labor village for rural primary schools. Other tasks such as spinning, weaving, twisting hemp, silk reeling, repairing and manufacturing simple agricultural tools, building grass sheds, tailoring and dyeing rough cloth clothes, socks, etc. are not seen in the exhibits. Among them, spinning and weaving may be due to a lack of equipment, but washing clothes and mending socks do not depend on equipment and are also neglected, which is a major shortcoming of this exhibition.

(2) According to the teaching rules of the labor course standard, the teaching materials should be selected to suit the local and current situation. The organization of teaching materials should be interconnected, and practice should enable children to "use both hands and brains" and "do" in "practice." Among all the exhibits, the ones that have the above-mentioned spirit are all the products of the Fujian Provincial No. 2 Primary School and the soybean research unit products of the Central University Experimental School of Nanjing City, and the large unit design products of Xingzhongmen Primary School going to the front line. All the products of the Fujian Provincial No. 2 Primary School are carried out consistently with the design of a large unit, so the level of its products is from shallow to deep, the process is natural, the raw materials of the products are selected in an orderly manner, and it can pay attention to local products. The structure of the export is quite intentional, and the degree of production required is very suitable for the physical and mental health of children. The work of the products includes things made by individuals and things made by the whole school, which is quite in line with the main points of the curriculum. Moreover, the exhibition is in order, and a detailed report of the process is attached, so that visitors can examine its educational value in addition to appreciation. Therefore, it can be said to be one of its representative products. The soybean research unit products of the Central University Experimental School start with the research of natural science, followed by the practice of agricultural affairs such as sowing, cultivation, intertillage, and harvesting, followed by the practice of household affairs such as smoking beans, making soy sauce, making tofu milk, and making tofu, and then followed by the craft practice of making soybean growth specimens, pod models, etc. All the processes, in addition to detailed written records, also have photographic records of step-by-step practice items, and the results of the practice clearly show the facility status of applied curriculum standards and teaching rules. Therefore, it can also be said to be one of the representative products. The model of going to the front line designed by Xingzhongmen Primary School in Nanjing City is from "strengthening the body and saving the country" - a small sports field, "enriching national power" - several factory prototypes, "expanding air defense" - an airport, - a grand array of soldiers and horses, "army, navy, and air force" - aircraft carriers and warships, etc., "return my rivers and mountains" - a map of the four northeastern provinces is covered, all the troops, horses, guns, vehicles, planes, fleets, trains, and all military equipment, light and heavy, and other naval and air force prototypes are numerous, or they are cut into outlines by 马口假and pasted with different outline paper with images of characters and horses, or made of thick paper, or made of this bar, or using waste. Originally unsystematic small pieces, but they can form a very meaningful design model, and various operations are also commensurate with the level of children. The national defense products displayed throughout the field are the best of their kind.

Ding Wenjiang Leaves Beijing for Ping

(Nanjing, November 21st) Ding Wenjiang left for Ping on the evening of the 11th to attend the annual meeting of the Geology Society. After the meeting, he and Weng Wenhao will investigate the geology of Shanxi.

President Mościcki's Thirty Years of Scientific Contributions

(Warsaw Correspondence) Since the renowned British chemist Crook issued a warning in 1889 that the Chilean nitrate deposits were nearing depletion, farmers and industrialists have been greatly alarmed. The only natural source of nitrogen needed for the chemical industry was potassium nitrate. If the source were cut off and artificial manufacturing were used instead, the cost would be too high, which would cause the economic situation of the industry to be difficult to salvage. Fortunately, the brilliant Ignacmojciki (the current President of Poland), while serving as an assistant in the Physics Department of Fuforog University, invented the use of high-voltage electricity to directly synthesize oxygen and nitrogen. At the same time, he modified the original condenser to be made of glass, so that the voltage could be increased from 10,000 volts to 50,000 volts to complete the high-voltage synthesis of nitrogen (the glass condenser was also used by the Eiffel Tower radio station). In 1903, a nitric acid company was established in Fuforog, and Mościcki's invention was the extraction of anhydrous nitric acid from the air. From experimentation, it entered the industrialization period for the first time. In 1904, the Cracovie Academy of Sciences published Mościcki's paper on electrical insulation, and his reputation as a scientist began to flourish. In 1912, he quickly returned to Poland to take over the position of professor of physics and electrochemistry at the Swow Institute of Technology. Subsequently, when the European War broke out, he had to work hard to improve the Polish petroleum industry. The Motiau Academy was also established at this time. He made many improvements to the methods of petroleum extraction and refining and obtained patents for the production of gasoline and gaseous carbohydrates, etc. This is only a small part of his chemical inventions. In 1922, part of High Silesia and the Golian plant were returned to Poland. Mościcki uniquely dispatched new methods to increase the annual production of the plant from 70,000 tons of diluted compounds to 170,000 tons. This progress in the chemical industry must be regarded as one of Mościcki's greatest successes. After being elected president in 1926, his heavy duties were enough to hinder the progress of his scientific work, but he was still able to take time to build a large-scale chemical factory, namely a diluted compound factory, in the city of Mościce. Poland relied on Mościcki's greatest efforts to complete the above two factories, so that the country was not only not excluded in the international diluted compound market, but instead jumped to become one of the countries with the most surplus. Furthermore, he built a device that, under physical and chemical conditions, regardless of cities and villages, allowed people in cities to breathe fresh air. With Mościcki's thirty years of continuous efforts and struggles, the results obtained are not only beneficial to Poland, but also to the whole world. Moreover, as the head of state who holds the highest position and the most burdensome duties in a country, he can still calmly devote himself to science, which is rare and valuable. This is a brief overview of Mościcki's contributions to science.

Casting of Phonetic Chinese Character Copper Molds Begins

National Textbooks to be Changed

Li Tan Investigates the Situation of Copper Mold Casting in Shanghai

Simplified Characters Drafted by Qian Xuantong to be Published

Mandarin in Beijing and Shanghai Spreads Naturally without Promotion

(Beijing Express News) Li Jinxi and Wang Yi, members of the National Language Unification Committee of the Ministry of Education, went to Beijing from Ping on the 22nd of last month at the invitation of Minister Wang Shijie. On the 26th, a meeting was held in the ministry to discuss the copper molds for phonetic Chinese characters and the issue of simplified characters. It was decided that Li and Wang would go to Shanghai to investigate the casting of copper molds, as reported in the previous newspaper. Yesterday (the 8th), Li and Wang returned to Ping from Beijing. The reporter specially interviewed Mr. Li, and the conversation is as follows:

National Textbooks and Newspapers to be Changed

The motive for the Ministry of Education to carry out these two matters this time is actually because the country is in danger, and the majority of the people lack national consciousness, national concepts, and common sense of citizenship. If something happens one day, it will be difficult to resist materially, and it is feared that they will eventually fall into ruin spiritually. The central government has decided to allocate funds to quickly implement short-term compulsory education, shortened to about two years, and force people to attend school. Adult education will be carried out as usual by local mass education institutions. However, short-term teaching must remove the obstacles of difficult-to-recognize and difficult-to-write characters, otherwise there will be no practical effect. Therefore, the textbooks and general readings for compulsory education and mass education in the future will uniformly annotate the Chinese characters with phonetic symbols, that is, use the lead

characters cast by this copper mold for typesetting. If the phonetic symbols are fixedly linked to the Chinese characters, the labor of annotating each character will be saved during drafting, and the typesetter will also get two benefits in one fell swoop. It saves money and is also beautiful. If bookstores do not use this lead character for typesetting, they will not be approved and will be prohibited from selling. Newspapers across the country will also be required by the government to implement the ministry order of the Republic of China's 19th year, and must at least open a special column to print mass readings with this lead character.

General Situation of Copper Mold Casting Investigation in Shanghai

If this copper mold is finely made, the latest [mother mold machine] must be purchased and the copper plate engraved. Within three years, the number 3, 4, and 5 lead characters can be made for application, but the cost will be more than 100,000 yuan. Because the Chinese characters must be changed to rectangular, occupying one-third of the lead character, and phonetic symbols are added next to it to form a square, so that the typesetting does not take up too much space between the lines, the length will not increase, and the book price will be commensurate with the purchasing power of the public. Therefore, it must be written and engraved as a whole, and the project is relatively large. If old methods such as wood lead engraving or photographic copper plate are used, the cost can be saved more, but it is not as fine and deep as the mother mold copper plate and is not durable. As for rough manufacturing, the better ones among the imitation Song long-body characters of various families are taken, and phonetic symbols are arranged next to them for combined casting. Then the copper mold lead characters can be completed in half a year, and the cost is the most economical. Now, because of the urgent need for printing and engraving, this method will probably be adopted. Because this copper mold lead character is to be promoted to the publishing and printing industries across the country, it is based on the principle of not allowing patents. Therefore, Shanghai merchants cannot undertake it unconditionally, and the government must raise considerable funds.

Simplified Characters to be Announced in Two Batches during Spring and Summer Vacations

If simplified characters also need to be cast into lead character copper molds, Shanghai merchants are willing to undertake them. Magazine circles, such as The Analects and Taibai, are also automatically casting them. Mr. Lin Yutang and I talked about the Hanwen Regular Script lead characters used in The World. The Shanliangyou Company is also selecting and casting simplified characters, but on the one hand, they all hope that the Ministry of Education will officially recognize them so that the application can be popularized without obstruction. Before returning to Ping, it was agreed with the ministry that the National Language Committee would compile a [Practical Simplified Character List] and publish the first batch during the spring vacation, which are commonly used characters for children and the public. The second batch of simplified characters that have been circulating will be published during the summer vacation, all drafted by Mr. Qian Xuantong, and the style will be determined. In the future, they can also be used as simplified character practice templates and lead character copper mold templates. After the simplified character list is published, the textbook textbooks can be directly used as the main text. If the traditional characters need to be recognized, they will be annotated next to the new word column. Students who use simplified characters in the student association examination and school entrance examination papers will not be crossed out. As for the use of official documents, it still needs to be passed by the Central Executive Council. After this table is completed, it will still be made into a [Simplified Character Spectrum] within a year and a half according to the resolution of the National Language Committee's standing meeting. In the future, a special committee may be formed by the Ministry of Education to make final supplementary decisions. Also, the name of simplified characters cannot be called [Simplified Characters]. Simplified Characters are a kind of character invented by Lao Naixuan at the end of the Qing Dynasty. Simplified characters are still Chinese characters, but only the strokes are reduced. The Shanghai publishing industry may call them [Handwritten Characters], which is also an example of the same reality with a different name.

Impressions of Education in Beijing, Shanghai, and Wuxi

Mr. Li also talked about his impressions of this trip to the south. He said that Mr. Wang and I visited the experimental area of the Wuxi Provincial Education Institute. Laborers' huts (rickshaw drivers, female workers, and poor families) are all equipped with educational facilities, and they are working very hard. However, everywhere I feel that the writing tools are not good, and it is very difficult for them to read books and newspapers. There are many fishing families in Taihu Lake. Because they live in boats and have no fixed mooring, education has not yet been possible. Standard Mandarin is no longer a problem. Because of the natural trend of transportation, such as Beijing, Shanghai, and Guangzhou radio broadcasts, and sound machines are everywhere, what you hear is Mandarin. I have not traveled south for twelve years, and I only learned that Mandarin has been spreading naturally without promotion. However, the use of phonetic symbols is not very strong in various schools, because the teachers are not familiar with it. In short, to revitalize the nation, we must rationalize the writing tools. This is a major issue in education.

Bureau of Education Stipulates Agricultural Busy Season Holidays to Facilitate Elementary School Students in Rural Areas

From the Beginning of Summer to the Grain in Ear, and from the Autumn Equinox to the Frost's Descent

Schools May Grant Holidays Based on Circumstances

The municipal elementary schools in the rural areas of this city have submitted a request to the Bureau of Education to urgently respond to the agricultural busy season and change the holidays. The bureau believes that the crops in the rural areas of this city are mostly vegetables, cotton, and wheat, which are slightly different from those in general rural areas. Granting holidays during the agricultural busy season is not a universal need for all schools. Therefore, it was decided to convene a meeting of more than ten principals of elementary schools in the rural areas to discuss and decide that June in the first half of the year, that is, from the Beginning of Summer to the Grain in Ear, and October in the second half of the year, that is, from the Autumn Equinox to the Frost's Descent, are the agricultural busy season. Whether each school needs an agricultural busy season holiday is determined by each school based on its own circumstances. If a holiday is required, it should be submitted to the bureau for approval ten days in advance. The holiday should not exceed two weeks, and a make-up class plan must be submitted. It is said that all elementary schools in the rural areas will be notified to comply.

Various Groups Held Enthusiastic Farewell Party Last Night

Before Departing, Encouraging Young People to Save the Country Through Self-Reliance

Since the news of Mr. Xue Guangqian's study in Italy spread, various groups in this city believed that Mr. Xue had been serving the community for many years with outstanding achievements. Those who attended the meeting included Bureau Chief of the Municipal Bureau of Education Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Yu Ming, Municipal Party Committee Member Tao Baichuan, Chen Kecheng of the Municipal Government, Zhu Xuefan of the General Labor Union, Huang Zhaoxiong of the Municipal Education Association, Kang Xuanyi of the University Education Association, Ren Xianqun of the University League, Chen Jicheng of the Secondary Education Association, Xu Zexiang, Sun Xiaolou of Soochow University, Du Gang of the Municipal Education Bureau, Wang Longzhang of the Modern Thought Society, and representatives from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Citizens' Federation, the Chinese General Assembly of Nari, the China Cultural Construction Association, the Chinese Stenography Association, the Private School Advancement Association, the Chongming Shanghai Students Association, and various schools and newspaper agencies, totaling more than 300 people. If the nation and clan want to continue and prosper, it is not enough for the youth of the country to break through obstacles and strive for self-reliance to achieve this goal. It is said that Mr. Xue will set sail on the Contifudi ship and will board the ship at the New Customs Pier at 8:00 tonight and leave the port tomorrow morning.

Lixin Accounting Evening School Opens

Lixin Accounting School, located at 190 Ningbo Road, this city, was founded by accountant Dr. Pan Xulun. Since its establishment, it has been seven and a half years. It is divided into two departments: correspondence and evening school. The correspondence department enrolls students all year round and can enroll at any time. The evening school department is one session every six months. The fourteenth session has ended, and the fifteenth session will open on February 11th. The classes offered by the evening school include: 1. Introductory and elementary accounting courses, 2. Advanced accounting courses (the above two courses are taught in both Chinese and English groups), 3. Bank accounting course, 4. Cost accounting course, 5. Auditing course, 6. Company accounting course, 7. Government accounting course, etc. It is said that the school, in view of the large number of applicants for admission in previous sessions and the limited school site and narrow classrooms, although it has tried its best to accommodate nearly 400 people, there are still dozens of applicants who are not admitted. Therefore, in order to remedy this regret, several large classrooms have been newly opened on the New China Bank building at the intersection of Jiangxi Road and Ningbo Road, and more classes have been opened to accommodate them. In addition, the class time of the evening school was originally from 7:00 pm to 9:00 pm every day. This time is quite inconvenient for students who have no duties after 5:00 pm. It is now heard that from this session onwards, an early class has been added, which starts at 5:30 pm and ends at 7:15 pm, so that students who have finished their duties in various agencies early can go to school first and then return home to rest. It is now heard that because the opening date of the school is approaching, the number of people who go to register for admission these days is very crowded, and the classes offered will soon be full.

New Female Tennis Player

Ms. Xia Lanzheng Passes Away

Ms. Xia Lanzheng, a new female tennis player, unfortunately passed away on the day of Lichun. There has often been a sigh of talent shortage in tennis in China, and there are even fewer women who engage in tennis and can achieve good results. With Ms. Xia's qualifications and efforts, if she had been given time, she would have been able to achieve great things. It is a pity that God did not grant her a long life, and she passed away. This is not only a major loss for the tennis world, but also a tragedy for the Chinese people. Ms. Xia was 19 years old and belonged to Siming. She lost her father early and had only her mother and two younger siblings. She was kind and approachable, extremely intelligent, excellent in character and learning, and always had a childish air about her. Because she had two small braids behind her, her friend Dong often jokingly called her the "Double-Braid Girl," which she never took offense to. While studying at the Chinese and Western Girls' School, she became very interested in tennis. At that time, she was invincible in the school, and teachers and friends all praised her as not being an ordinary person. Sure enough, she showed her strength as soon as she started, and served as the city's representative to participate in the National Games. Last year, she won the open singles championship. Ms. Xia was not satisfied with this and still practiced hard every day. For the convenience of practice, she transferred to the Public Concession Girls' School last autumn, and her practice became even more diligent.

Ms. Xia was a member of the Chinese Sports Association. She usually liked to play against men during practice, very much in the style of Helen Wills of the United States. In addition to hard practice, she often sought advice from Sun Linfang and Zhou Guanjun. Seeing her talent, Sun and others had high expectations for her, and guided her wholeheartedly, sparing no effort. Ms. Xia was extremely intelligent, and after basic training, she progressed very quickly. Her forehand and backhand strokes were fast and accurate, her posture was graceful, and she had a good foundation, which was beyond the reach of other female tennis players.

Dr. Tu Kaiyuan admired her character very much, and Ms. Xia often asked him for advice. When the open singles was held last year, Dr. Tu put in a lot of effort and insisted on her practicing every morning, and personally supervised and instructed her in every battle. As a result, she won the championship. Since then, the two have become more and more intimate. Last winter, Dr. Tu went to further his studies again. Before leaving, he was reluctant to leave, but in the end he thought it was just a short separation. How could he have expected that one separation would become eternal? The ocean is vast and the paths of life and death are different. When Dr. Tu heard the news, he must have regretted having made this trip. Fate is so tricky.

Ms. Xia's illness was not fatal, but she had a small boil on the back of her neck, which was accidentally infected by dirt during a haircut, causing blood poisoning and making it impossible to recover. She passed away on the day of the Spring Festival, when the earth was reviving, and in the sound of firecrackers, this promising young woman fell asleep forever. Alas!

Commercial News

Financial Swap Approaching a Massive Short Squeeze

Gold Market's Floating Long Positions Collapse

丨Continuing Downward Slide of Eleven Yuan丨

The gold market is under the massive threat of a short squeeze. Buyers find it extremely difficult to rally. The swap is on the verge of expiring, and the long positions are even more fearful, causing floating long positions to collapse. The foreign exchange market fuels the selling pressure, and the downward trend is quite severe, gradually weakening. The large long positions are also shaken, and the price has fallen to a low of 41.7 yuan before slightly stabilizing. In the morning, the London and New York silver markets were flat, and the forward silver price remained almost unchanged. London spot gold rose by one penny. Reports indicate that the Silver Price Research Committee, jointly formed by the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, and Jinling University, announced that to save the declining industry and commerce, it is necessary to reform the currency system and devalue silver to the level of 1931 (note that the foreign exchange rate in that year was close to one shilling and one penny, and the US dollar was around 20 yuan). This news boosted confidence, and off-exchange trading opened higher, rising to around 55 yuan. The Central Bank's official exchange rate was announced, with the British pound flat and the US dollar rising. The customs gold unit also rose by one li, and the standard price for the gold standard was 965.1 yuan. The morning opened high, but the foreign exchange market remained strong, and large short sellers exerted pressure, causing the price to fall immediately. Upon learning that the HSBC's official exchange rate showed the British pound rising by 1.25 and the US dollar rising by 3.125, selling pressure surged, pushing the price to around 50 yuan. Bargain hunting activities eased the decline. However, the foreign exchange market became overly relaxed, and although the silver equalization tax remained unchanged, the short sellers continued to exert pressure, causing the long positions to collapse. Despite some struggles, the selling pressure intensified, and the 50 yuan mark could not be maintained. The trend was extremely weak, and the market slightly stabilized at noon. In the afternoon session, the price fell due to the liquidation of long positions by the large firm Fuchang, but the initial report of a decrease in Indian silver by four annas led to a rebound. Banks continued to offer positions, but the market remained loose and lacked support. Floating long positions took the opportunity to close out their positions and pushed the price down to 41.3 yuan. The domestic market of banks stabilized, and there was some support after the low, gradually rebounding. However, the second report of an increase in Indian silver by one anna caused the market to turn sideways. The trend is still difficult to revive, and with the swap approaching, the situation is extremely unfavorable for the long positions. Large firms continue to arbitrage, and the future is not optimistic. The daily market situation is recorded as follows:

The morning opening was 954.3 yuan, slightly higher than the previous close by 0.9 yuan. It then went to 954.7 yuan. Foreign Exchange Continues to Loosen

Situation More Peaceful Than Gold Market

Chinese Merchants Sell U.S. Dollars and Buy British Pounds

Yesterday, according to foreign dispatches, London big bars were flat for both near and far terms. New York silver prices were unchanged. Monte Rio forward silver prices rose and fell slightly. London spot gold rose one penny. The British pound rose 1.25 against the U.S. dollar, and the U.S. dollar rose 6.25 against the British pound. The British pound fell 7 pounds against the French franc, and the U.S. dollar rose 1.625 against the French franc. The foreign exchange market opened in the morning with recent selling prices, the British exchange rate at one shilling and five pence and seventy-five hundredths, and the U.S. exchange rate at 36 yuan and six hundred and twenty-five ten-thousandths, compared to last Saturday's noon closing, the British pound was flat and the U.S. dollar was tighter by six hundred and twenty-five ten-thousandths. The Central Bank's official exchange rate was announced, the British pound was flat and the U.S. dollar rose by six hundred and twenty-five ten-thousandths, and the customs gold unit rose by one li, with no significant impact. The banks' appetite was not strong, and the Chinese merchants' intake was still weak, and the market loosened as soon as it opened. Upon learning of HSBC's official exchange rate announcement, the British pound rose by 1.25 and the U.S. dollar rose by 1.325. Although the banks did some hedging, the process was already tight. After entering the market, Sassoon and the banks mutually offered positions. The silver equalization tax was announced, and although it was not changed, due to a lack of support, the situation continued to loosen. Although the banks did some hedging, they were unable to sustain the market due to oversupply. In the afternoon session, banks offered near-term positions and bought far-term positions, and the initial report of a decrease in Indian silver by four annas made the situation more peaceful. Although the banks continued to supply, the Chinese merchants' psychology was extremely weak, and their intake was not strong, so the selling pressure was not intense, and the market was loose but not strong. The final situation was mediocre, and the recent selling price at the closing was 1s. 5 875d for the British exchange rate and 36.4375 yuan for the U.S. exchange rate. Compared to last Saturday, the British pound was firmer by 1.25 and the U.S. dollar was firmer by 3.125. Financial Sector Remains Quiet After Reopening

Reflecting This Year's Sluggish Market Sentiment

Yesterday was Monday. Normally, banks would be busy with opening and settling accounts. However, due to the Lunar New Year holiday, the financial sector only operated for half a day. In the afternoon, there was nothing to do as usual, so business was quite quiet. In addition, the money market was poor, and most firms adopted a contractionary policy and were unwilling to engage in extensive trade. Therefore, the market situation across various sectors remained largely unchanged. Although interbank lending rates were tight, they did not rise. The morning market rate was only 6%, similar to the previous day. The premium rate was added, and because there was no afternoon market, there was no market price. In terms of bill transactions, morning transfers amounted to over 1.7 million, with new transactions of over 400,000. The source of funds included 150,000 in silver from Ningbo and Tianjin, with no outflow. There was no lending activity against foreign goods, only 300,000 was repaid. In terms of bank settlements, foreign banks settled over 900,000 in bills, 2.8 to 2.9 million in various goods, foreign exchange, and miscellaneous loans, 1.4 million in rice loans, and over 400,000 in special remittances, with 100,000 going into warehouses. Chinese banks settled over 1 million in bills, 2.6 to 2.7 million in various goods, foreign exchange, taxes, and miscellaneous loans, over 1.2 million in rice loans, over 500,000 in special remittances, over 400,000 in telegraphic transfers, with inflows and outflows balanced. Japanese banks settled 500,000 to 600,000 in bills, 800,000 to 900,000 in various goods and miscellaneous loans, over 400,000 in special remittances, and 200,000 went out of warehouses. Money shops settled 5.5 to 5.6 million in foreign government bonds, over 1.2 million in premium loans, over 200,000 in inter-city remittances, and over 100,000 in cash. In addition, the total number of bills exchanged at the local clearing house on the 11th was 5,836,719.96 silver dollars, including 4,094,149.03 silver dollars and 1,742,570.93 silver dollars in remittances.

Subsidiary Coin Market Prices Fall

Yesterday, the market prices of various subsidiary coins generally declined. Jiangnan small silver coins were priced at 820 yuan in the morning, down 10 yuan from the previous day, with 3,000 units traded. Guangdong small silver coins were priced at 755 yuan, down 3.8 yuan from the previous day, with 45,000 units traded. Copper coins rose by 2,000 cash, to 319,000 cash, with 51,040 strings traded, equivalent to 16,000 silver dollars. All prices were suspended in the afternoon.

Securities and Bonds Fall Across the Board

The 23rd Customs Bond Alone Rises by Four Yuan

Abnormal State of the Government Bond Market

Yesterday, the interbank lending rate at the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange was 6%, slightly higher by 4%. The environment was stable as before, but sentiment seemed softer. Most firms were selling, except for the 23rd Customs Bond, which was actively absorbed. At a time when various market prices were falling sharply, the 23rd Customs Bond soared according to its book value, rising by over four yuan in one session and then being suspended from trading. This extremely abnormal and distorted state was rare. There were various rumors in the market, but no confirmed information. Some said that the Ministry of Finance intended to completely redeem the 23rd Customs Bond and issue 20 million yuan of the 24th Customs Bond, with the principal repayment halved compared to the 23rd Customs Bond. This argument seemed unlikely, because the government would first need to raise several million yuan to redeem nearly 10 million yuan of the 23rd Customs Bond, which was already circulating in the market, before issuing the 24th Customs Bond. Moreover, there was no prior indication of this measure, so it was not credible. Others said that because the amount of the 23rd Customs Bond circulating in the market was very small, it was easy for capitalists to monopolize it. This measure has many precedents, but at the same time, other bonds should also rise, not diverge so greatly. Still others said that in view of the favorable terms of the 23rd Customs Bond, financial firms sold other bonds and bought the 23rd Customs Bond, thus causing a squeeze. This reasoning seemed more plausible. Currently, the 23rd Customs Bond is at 90%, and the March futures market price is only 9 yuan different from the par value. What is the underlying reason? It will be clear within a day or two. The trend and future direction may be upward due to the surge in the 23rd Customs Bond. Yesterday's market was extremely chaotic. When the market opened, numbers 4, 5, and 11, etc. were selling, and various bonds were falling sharply. When the 23rd Customs Bond was auctioned, the atmosphere in the market suddenly tightened. The opening price rose by 2 yuan. At that time, numbers 11, 23, 47, and 48 were the most active buyers. The market price jumped and rose sharply, and in an instant, it rose by more than 4 yuan and was suspended from trading. In the next session, sellers were still very active, and the market price fell slightly by 2 to 3, 6 to 7 corners. The 23rd Customs Bond was temporarily suspended due to tracking. As a result, except for the 23rd Customs Bond, which rose to the limit, the rest fell. The total transaction volume was 16,401,000 yuan.
